The Tragedy of Starving People Looting Grain in Nancheng 66

Villagers Riot; Many Casualties

Nanchang Correspondence: Jiangxi Province suffered from insect pests, drought, and communist bandits last year, resulting in harvests of less than 50% of normal levels throughout the province. This year, the scarcity of rice and grain and the number of starving people are unprecedented. Everywhere, there are incidents of preventing rice and grain from leaving the area, as well as trends of people snatching rice and seizing food. Recently, grain merchants Luo Yunbiao and Jiang Fengzhou from the provincial capital purchased over 1,200 dan of rice and grain in Shangtang Market, Nancheng County, and loaded it onto 22 bamboo rafts for transport downstream. Fearing that starving people would loot the grain along the way, the merchants requested over 60 armed soldiers from the Second Squad of the First Company of the First Battalion of police to protect the rafts and prevent accidents. Unexpectedly, when they reached the river below Wuhu Village in the 44th district of the county, a group of starving people suddenly stopped the rafts from going downstream, claiming that local food supplies had run out and they were experiencing famine. They demanded to purchase 30% of the grain at a reduced price (estimated at 300-400 dan) before allowing it to pass. The two grain merchants, Luo and Jiang, were prevented from moving their grain and went ashore to negotiate with Ning Jinliang, the head of the 44th district, for several days without any result. On June 1st, the traditional Dragon Boat Festival, a huge crowd of villagers gathered at the river below Wuhu Village to watch the dragon boat races. Seeing this situation, Luo and Jiang thought the villagers had come to loot the grain. They went ashore from the rafts to explain, but the conversation escalated into a conflict. The villagers suddenly grabbed Jiang Fengzhou and started beating him. Luo Yunbiao, fearing that he would be next, jumped into the river. Since Luo could not swim, the villagers chased him in the water, and he cried for help, asking the police squad to open fire. The soldiers on the rafts, not knowing the full situation, immediately opened fire with live ammunition, killing Quan Fufeng, Yang Jiaoguan, Xu Wufu, and Zhu Gousi on the spot, and seriously injuring Quan Sanlu and Xu Zhixian. At that time, the villagers were unaware that many had been shot. After explanations from the Shangtang Police Station, Luo and Jiang were handed over to Inspector Xie for custody. Afterwards, the villagers learned of the deaths and injuries, and a mob of two to three thousand people gathered in anger. In addition to destroying the home of Li Jueqiao, who was in partnership with Luo and Jiang in the grain business, they demanded from the Shen and Zhang Commissioners sent by the county magistrate (1) that Luo and Jiang be executed on the spot; (2) that the detained 1,200 dan of grain be sold at a low price as compensation for the dead; and (3) that Li Jueqiao be arrested and executed. The Shen and Zhang Commissioners agreed to consider the demands and were trying to disperse the crowd when over a thousand more villagers arrived, chanting that Jiang and Luo had to be killed. They rushed into the Shangtang Police Station and dragged out Luo Yunbiao and Jiang Fengzhou, beating them to death. This case resulted in a total of six deaths and two injuries, another tragedy amidst the grain shortage. The Civil Affairs Department received a telegram from the Nancheng County Magistrate yesterday reporting the incident and has reportedly dispatched personnel together with the Security Department to thoroughly investigate. (June 9th)

Case of French Sailor Raping Chinese Woman in Qingdao 67

Municipal Government Lodges Strong Protest

French Consulate Apologizes to Municipal Government

Perpetrator Handed Over to French Consulate in Shanghai for Handling

Qingdao Correspondence: Qingdao is a treaty port with a mix of Chinese and foreigners. Foreigners, relying on consular jurisdiction, often bully the Chinese. Yesterday, a sailor from the French ship “Lifu Liqi Linke” forcibly dragged a Chinese woman, Dong Zhang, onto the ship in broad daylight and raped her almost to death. The citizens were extremely indignant upon hearing this. The details of the incident and the negotiations are as follows:

Details of the Incident: At 11:00 AM on the 10th of this month, Zhang, the wife of Dong Zelin, a worker at the Sifang Dakang Textile Mill, who was about 25 or 26 years old, was strolling with a neighbor near the Dagang pier. As they walked along the coast of godown F, a sailor from the French ship “Lifu Liqi Linke” came ashore and forcibly dragged Zhang onto the ship. Although Zhang desperately cried for help, there were few pedestrians on the pier, and no one came to her assistance. The neighbor, seeing this situation, panicked and ran away. Fortunately, a coolie saw the incident from afar and rushed to report it to the police post, which in turn reported it to the sub-station. The patrol officer of the sub-station immediately led a police escort to investigate. However, the sailors firmly closed the cabin doors and ignored the police's calls. Unable to do otherwise, the police went to see the captain and informed him of the incident. Accompanied by the captain, they went to the sailors' quarters and opened the door. Several French sailors were inside. Zhang was lying naked on the bed, moaning incessantly, having been gang-raped and on the verge of death.

Negotiations: After receiving the report, the Public Security Bureau immediately sent Inspector-General Andre, a German, to negotiate with the captain and reported the matter to the Municipal Government. Upon receiving the report, the Municipal Government, in addition to ordering the port authorities to detain the ship and not allow it to load cargo, also instructed the Third Section Chief Wu Zifeng to lodge a strong protest with the French Consul. Today (the 11th), Public Security Bureau Andre, along with Paling & Co. General Manager Pei Mengshi, Chinese lawyers Song Chunfang and Li Han, and French acting Consul Tatalingfu, went to the scene to conduct an on-site investigation and interrogated the sailors. The evidence was conclusive and undeniable. The French acting Consul admitted that the sailor had indeed committed improper behavior and would take custody of him and apologize to the Municipal Government in writing.

Subsequent Handling: The French acting Consul has stated to the Municipal Government that the sailor involved will be handed over to the French Consul-General in Shanghai to be severely punished according to French law to deter future incidents. As for Dong Zhang, the shipowner will be responsible for compensating her for her loss of reputation as a settlement. (June 11th)

Troop Rotation of Xiang and Jiang and Public Security in Chaozhou and Meizhou 68

Shantou Correspondence: Xiang Hanping's troops have been ordered to come to Chaozhou and Meizhou to be stationed and are responsible for suppressing the Zhu-Mao communist bandits on the Fujian-Jiangxi border. The two brigades of Xiang’s division, led by Zhang Da and Zhang Ruigui, have arrived in Shantou last week and have gone to various counties in the upper reaches of the Han River to be stationed. The officers of the division headquarters also arrived in Shantou on the 7th and began working in Shantou. According to Li Heling, the political training director of the division, Xiang Shizhang (Division Commander Xiang) has sores and is now recuperating in Guangzhou and will come to Shantou with Chief of Staff Ye Minyu soon. He also said that the entire force of the Zhu-Mao communist bandits is about 5,000 men, and their main force is in Tao Wu County, Jiangxi, and only a small part of them came to Pingyuan. After the main force is stationed in Meixian, it will not be difficult to suppress them. Zhang Da's brigade has now completed the handover of defense duties in Meixian. Brigade Commander Mao Weishou passed through Shantou on the 6th on his way back to the province. It is reported that Zhu and Mao have fled back to Xunwu and towards the hinterland of Jiangxi Province.

Li Mingguang, a local communist in Fengshun, recently led bandits to invade Jiuhe, wanting to attack the Xihuang area along the Han River. They were repelled by the military police and fled back to the Yangmeikeng and Shanglinkeng villages in the first district. Another group of local communists is causing trouble in the areas of Wuhua, Meilin, Anliu, Liyujiang, and Shangshan, confronting the guard team in Xikeng and Xiashan. Another force led by Gu Zaicun, about a thousand men, is the most rampant. On the morning of the 1st of this month, they invaded Chaoan from Fengshun Huang磜 in three routes: one route attacked Wuquan from the east, one route attacked Tiandong from Shitain, and one route attacked Fengshuwai from Juxi. Each route had about three to four hundred bandits. When the bandits came, they planted flags all over the mountains to create a false impression of strength, directly targeting the Dengtang district. At that time, the guard teams stationed in Wuquan and Tiandong fought fiercely with the bandits for half an hour. Due to being outnumbered, the bandits reached Fengshuwai at 1:00 PM on the 1st, only 20 li away from Chaoan city. Ruan Sheqing, the magistrate of Chaoan County, transferred police teams from Shangpu and other places to Dengtang to intercept them. When the bandits arrived at Fengshuwai, the telephone lines between Chaoan and Dengtang had already been cut by the bandits. The bandits and police fought fiercely for a long time. When Zhang Ruigui's brigade arrived at Chaoan City on the 3rd and cooperated with the police teams to suppress the bandits towards Tiandongxu, the local communists saw that reinforcements had arrived and fled back to Fengshun via Shitain, Juxi, and Gaoshan. (June 8th)

Kunshan 69

Extortionist Arrested on the Spot: The family of Ma Rusong, a villager in Baijiacun outside the East Gate, is quite well-off, leading to them being targeted by bandits. After receiving the letter, Ma was extremely frightened. On that day, he sent someone to the agreed-upon location, but they did not encounter anyone. Unexpectedly, the bandits sent two people to demand the money in person. Helpless, Ma had already taken refuge with relatives, so the bandits could not do anything. At 2:00 PM on the twelfth, the two bandits came to demand the money in person again. Ma's uncle, Shuyun, immediately reported to the First Police Station of the Public Security Bureau. After receiving the report, Patrol Officer Yu Fuxin, together with members of the Chamber of Commerce and armed members of the First Branch, rushed to arrest them. By the time they arrived, the bandits had already learned of their arrival and fled from the house, but they were captured by the members of the Chamber of Commerce. Suzhou 71

Lu Gengrong Case Scheduled for Trial; Huang and Lu's Love Affair the Main Focus: Lu Gengrong re-appealed to the Supreme Court, which in the previous month ruled that the case be sent back to the High Court for retrial. Case of Fratricide Occurs in Hengjing Township: Zhou Ye, a resident of Hengjing Township, 45 years old, was killed by his son, Wei Lin, 25 years old. On the afternoon of the previous day (the 12th), Wei Lin demanded money from his father without success, and killed him with a millstone. The murderer was handed over to the city yesterday (the 13th).

Telephone Problems Occur in Sumu: In addition to Suzhou city, the Suzhou Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications has three rural areas within its communication area: Lumu, Waikuatang, and Mudu. However, communication between Mudu and Suzhou city has only been available for three months. When the bureau first laid the telephone lines to Mudu, it submitted to the Ministry of Communications for approval a regulation stipulating that calls from the city to Mudu would be charged five cents each time, but calls from Mudu to Suzhou city would not be charged. At the time, there was no such announcement to the telephone users in Mudu. Now, the residents of Mudu are opposing the rule of charging five cents extra for calls from the city to Mudu. They elected a user representative, Wang Shujie, the director of the People's Education Hall, to negotiate with the telephone bureau, but the bureau said that the fee was already on record with the ministry and could not be canceled, so there was no result. Telephone users in Mudu have therefore refused to pay their monthly telephone fees. The telephone bureau may cut off telephone lines to Mudu on the 16th of this month. After the lines are cut, they plan to submit a report to the Ministry of Communications, stating the circumstances and requesting an appropriate resolution.

Artist Attempts Suicide and is Rescued: Ji Zongyu, a 22-year-old artist from Jiaxing, Zhejiang, who worked at the Wuxi Advertising Agency, came to Suzhou the previous day (the 12th) and stayed in room number 14 of the Lao Sutai Hotel outside the Changmen Gate. Due to economic pressure, he had thoughts of suicide and secretly swallowed a bottle of sleeping pills. The hotel tea room staff discovered this and sent him to Suyong Hospital for treatment. After an operation by Director Gu, he regained consciousness. It was then learned that Ji had sent a quick letter to his friend Wang in the Wuxi Telegraph Bureau before coming to Suzhou, saying that he had something important to discuss and hoped that his brother could come to Suzhou quickly. After receiving the letter, Wang reported it to the advertising agency, and Director Zhang came to Suzhou with him to visit him at the hospital. According to Director Zhang, Ji's suicidal thoughts were not due to economic pressure, but because of a failed romance.

Progress in Urban Construction: Since the main roads and major bridges in the urban area of this county have been successively demolished and rebuilt, the traffic flow has been much more convenient. Although Changshou Bridge and Rihui Bridge outside the city are on branch roads, the traffic flow is also very heavy, so the district office also plans to demolish and rebuild them. Construction on Rihui Bridge began on the 10th. Daqiao Street has been in disrepair for a long time and is quite uneven, so it is necessary to repair it. Wuxi 73

County Government's Measures to Prevent Robberies: Recently, robberies have occurred frequently inside and outside the city. In order to ensure local safety, Magistrate Sun Zuji specially formulated four measures to prevent robberies yesterday and issued instructions to the Public Security Bureau to relay them to all sub-bureaus for compliance. The measures are as follows: (1) When a robbery occurs, the victim should try to report it to the local police or public security agency as soon as possible. Those with telephones should use them so that the Public Security Bureau can implement emergency measures in the shortest possible time. The telephone numbers of the relevant public security agencies should be recorded and memorized so that they can be reported immediately and avoid panic. (2) If the victim is trapped and unable to report the robbery at the time, the neighbors should report it on their behalf, according to the principle of mutual assistance. (3) If it is not convenient to report a robbery at the time, it should be reported directly to the public security agency or the district office within 24 hours of the incident, and the relevant agencies should immediately investigate and report it to the superior agency. (4) Victims and neighbors who violate the above measures will be subject to appropriate punishment.

Widow Dies Tragically from Abortion: A widow surnamed Mao, residing near Mianhua Lane outside the West Gate of this county, was over forty years old and determined to remain chaste for many years. However, she was seduced by a Zhu, the owner of a neighboring wine and rice shop, who saw that Mao was still attractive despite her age. As a result, they had an affair, and she became pregnant. By now, she was five months pregnant and quite bulky. Mao, concerned about her reputation, asked a midwife to perform an abortion. Unfortunately, the surgery was not successful, and she died. Zhu, realizing that he had caused a disaster, immediately fled elsewhere.

Telephone Connection Between Nine Counties: Long-distance telephone service between nine counties, including Wuxi, Jiangning, Jurong, Danyang, Wujin, Yixing, Jintan, Liyang, and Zhenjiang, was initially used exclusively for military purposes. After the situation stabilized, it was converted to civilian use. Recently, Huang Yunzhen, the magistrate of Wuxian County, proposed to connect the long-distance telephone service of the nine counties to Wuxian. Wuxian only needs to connect to Wuxi from Wujin, and then to Wuxian from Wuxi. It can also connect to Wujiang and Changshu, which would greatly benefit the commerce and security of Wuxian and the other nine counties. He immediately wrote to Yao, Director of the Construction Bureau of this county, to seek his opinion. Yao immediately wrote back to endorse Huang's proposal and then submitted a report to the provincial government to connect the telephone service of the nine counties to Wuxian. After discussion, the provincial government approved it and ordered the Department of Construction to review the matter. Upon receiving the order, Director Sun has instructed Huang, the magistrate of Wuxian County, and Yao, the Director of the Construction Bureau of this county, to be informed that the connection is approved. The department will send personnel to Wuxi to install telephone equipment and then go to Suzhou to connect the lines.

Changzhou 74

Record of Wucheng Joint Defense Meeting: The party and government organs of Wujin and Jiangyin counties initiated a joint defense meeting held on the 12th in Jiaoxi Town. The following resolutions were made: (1) Establish the Wucheng Joint Defense Office; (2) The organization of the Joint Defense Office will use a committee system; (3) The number of committee members should not exceed 25; (4) The committee members will be limited to those produced by the governments of the two counties, the party departments of the two counties, the public security bureaus of the two counties, and the relevant district offices, district party departments, and public security sub-bureaus of the two counties, as well as the water police team, Jiaoxi Town Office, and Chamber of Commerce branch; (5) Seven standing committee members will be elected from the public security sub-bureaus of the fifth district of Jiangyin County, the public security sub-bureaus of the fifth district of Wujin County, the district offices of the fourth and fifth districts of Wujin County, the Jiaoxi Town Office, the Jiaoxi Chamber of Commerce branch, and the district office of the sixth district of Jiangyin County; (6) The location will be the Jiaoxi Chamber of Commerce branch in Wujin; (7) The funding will be provided by the party and government organs of the two counties for recurring expenses, and temporary expenses will be drawn from the defense funds of the two counties.

Robbery with Injury Occurs in Fourth District: The home of Jiang Baosun, the deputy head of Gaochang Township in the fourth district of Wuyi County, was suddenly robbed on the night of the 11th. Jiang Baosun was tied up by the robbers, burned with kerosene, and shot, leaving him in critical condition. Public funds, public property receipts, and his own title deeds and clothing were all burned. The cash and silver were looted. When the nearby defense corps arrived, the bandits had already fled. The defense corps of the fourth district reported the incident to the county, and the injured man was taken to Wujin Hospital for treatment.

Nantong 75

Provincial Police Team Divides the Northern Jiangsu Defense Zone: Because the bandits in northern Jiangsu are rampant, the provincial government has appointed Li Changjiang, the commander of the provincial police team, as the temporary bandit suppression commander of nine counties, including Tongru. Li has led the four battalions of his department to northern Jiangsu and has divided the defense zone. The first battalion, led by Xia Zhen, is stationed in Yancheng and Funing; the second battalion, led by Yang Wei, is stationed in Huangqiao; the third battalion is stationed in Rugao and Jingjiang; and the fourth battalion, led by Yu Shimei, is stationed in Nantong.

Implementing Rectification of the Industrial Special Police Team: The Department of Civil Affairs has ordered the governments of all counties to effectively rectify the Tongtai Haiqi Industrial Special Police Team, which has 40 teams. The tenth battalion is designated to be stationed in Haimen, the second battalion is stationed in Nantong, and the third battalion is stationed in Chengtan. Zhang Dong has been appointed as the supervisory committee member, and the standing committee members will be re-elected on the 20th.

Distribution of Land Tax for Public Security Use: The annual land tax for public security in Nantong is 60,000 yuan. After the county political meeting, the funds will be distributed as follows: 60% for the public security team and 40% for the public security bureau.

Water Police Fight Fiercely with Pirates: Zhu Bingzheng, the chief of the fourth district of the Wusong Water Police, ordered the team leaders of the 16th, 17th, and 18th teams to lead their officers to encircle and suppress pirates due to the rampant piracy. It is reported that on the morning of the previous day (the 11th), while patrolling the Changyinsha port, they learned that pirates were hiding in the Dongxingsha waters. They immediately went to suppress them and encountered two sailing boats with two masts and three masts, respectively. Hundreds of pirates opened fire and resisted arrest. The water police patrol ship fired back and surrounded the pirate ships. The pirates were fierce and did not retreat. The captain ordered to fire more than 20 rapid-fire shells, hitting a three-masted ship. More than 70 pirates were drowned. The pirates' momentum was greatly reduced. The two sides confronted each other for about four or five hours before the pirate ships were repelled by the police.

Bandits Burn and Loot the Yu Family in Sha Yi: On the evening of the 11th, six or seven bandits suddenly came to the Yu residence in Sha Yi of Li Guanyintang, carrying box guns and surrounding the residence. Fortunately, the Yu family heard the news and escaped. The bandits then entered the residence and looted clothing, ornaments, and 150 yuan worth of foreign yarn. Then they set fire to the residence, burning more than a dozen houses. They shouted slogans and distributed leaflets before escaping separately.

Jiangyin 76

Tragic Robbery in Shizhuang Lane, Rugao: Shizhuang Lane in Rugao is a large market with more than 50 members of the defense corps. Due to the large number of bandits, a company of county police is stationed there, making their strength still strong. At about 4:00 PM on the 11th, hundreds of bandits suddenly came and started a riot, setting fire to Beijie and Xijie. The police team could not resist, and seventy or eighty shops were burned. The fire was blazing, and the shouts of killing were endless. The fire gradually subsided at about 8:00 PM. Many innocent merchants and civilians were killed or injured. Reinforcements from Zhang Huanggang and other places arrived and the bandits retreated to the northwest. Residents of the area took Datong and Dada Jiang ships to Cheng to take refuge. On the 12th, hundreds of people lived around Beiwai. Xu Wancheng, the owner of a sugar shop, was injured in the arm and leg by stray bullets and was treated at Jiangyin Hospital.

Suspects Arrested in Western Suburbs: The bandits in Licheng and other townships in the western suburbs are gradually rampant. Xu Xiaochuan of the county police team led his team to patrol the Xishiqiao area and went to Licheng Township and Lichunli to search. On the previous day, Gao Ma, the wife of Gao Dasheng, who had already been executed, was arrested at Jiajia Dian. Cao, the wife of Gao Xiaosheng, was arrested at Wushu. When Ma was arrested, Xu Xiaochuan was slapped by her, causing her to be beaten and her hand injured. She was taken to the sixth division, but had no confession. Cao and others all claimed that they had worked in the Hongxing Yarn Factory in Chedaojiao, Shanghai, and had returned home the previous day. The Director of the Cao branch sent them to the headquarters for handling. In addition, Tai Bao, a bandit, was arrested by the first police station of the Taohua Public Security Bureau in Shaoyao Port, Ding Taosha, because Geng had committed a kidnapping case in Qingjiang Taixing. Geng was escorted to the county by the sixth branch on the 12th. Zhu A Si, from Zhulangtou Bridge, Lumu Township, was a counter-revolutionary and committed murder of an ox. He escaped from prison in the spring of this year and has not been arrested. He suddenly returned home on the 11th. Cao, the district chief of the district, learned that Zhu had escaped and arrested his mother, Zhu Wu, the village chief, Zhu Rongsheng, and villagers Cao Qilang, Liu Alang, and Zhu Shunsheng, and sent them to the county because they knew about the bandits but did not report them.

Zhenjiang 77

Development of Silkworm Egg Production Factory: Zhenjiang Shifang Silkworm Egg Production Factory was founded by Wang Yanong. Wang is engaged in the Shanghai banking industry and is dedicated to industry. His wife, Ms. Feng Shiying, and his wife's sister, Ms. Xiao Fang, graduated from Jiangsu Provincial Women's Sericulture School and have many years of experience in the sericulture industry. In 1928, they founded a seed production factory in Yaoshi Temple in Zhenjiang City as the fundamental plan for improving silkworm seeds. In recent years, the factory has been very successful, and the supply of Huitou brand silkworm seeds has exceeded demand. Last year, they purchased more than 200 acres of land in Gaozi and planted 50,000 to 60,000 mulberry trees. The future development of seed production is immeasurable.

Provincial Government Reforms Pawnshop Malpractices: The provincial government previously approved a public letter from the Provincial Party Rectification Committee stating that the cost of pawnshop ticket printing should be borne by the pawnshop itself, and the monthly interest should not exceed 0.5%. The provincial government replied yesterday that "the stamp tax on pawnshop tickets has always been borne by the pawnshop. The monthly interest rate has also been regulated. Those exceeding 5 days a month will be charged half a month's interest, and those exceeding 15 days will be charged a month's interest, which is already reduced compared to the previous month when those exceeding 5 days were charged a month's interest." The local court sentenced six kidnappers to death by firing squad. Six kidnappers, Zhu Lao Si, Zhang Chengcai, Zhong Ba Shou, Zhu Wensheng, Zhu Kaiyuan, and Zhong Changsheng, kidnapped the victim Shu Xiuchen in Yaojiaqiao, Shujiazhuang on February 18 this year and demanded a ransom of 150,000 yuan. After Zhu Lao Si negotiated with the family in Shanghai, the price was reduced to 15,000 yuan. Just as they were about to pay the money, the Zhenjiang Investigation Team found out about the incident and, together with the Shanghai Public Concession Police, arrested Zhu and the other six men and sent them to the court for trial. Zhu Lao Si confessed to kidnapping and extortion. The court confirmed the facts and sentenced them to death in accordance with the law. The provincial government approved the sentence. Yesterday morning (the 12th) at 5:00 AM, Zhu and the other six convicts were taken to the execution ground outside the North Gate and executed by firing squad.

Provincial Relief Institute Holds Commemoration: The 14th of this month is the first anniversary of the establishment of the Provincial Relief Institute. The institute held a commemorative ceremony at 2:00 PM on that day at Boxian Park outside the city. The Provincial Party Department, the various departments of the Provincial Government, and the local agencies were invited to participate. The handicrafts produced by the various centers were displayed in the Jinghui Hall near the venue for public viewing. Women, the elderly, the disabled, and vagrants from the various centers were present to perform and add to the festivities.

Yangzhou 78

Arresting Suspected Imposter Famine Representatives: Yesterday, on the afternoon of the 11th, a man named Wan Haijin, claiming to be a representative of famine victims from Tongxu County, Henan Province, arrived at the Public Security Bureau with a county-issued passport. He claimed that there were over 140 famine victims in Baotawan outside the city, requesting a stamp to facilitate travel to other counties. The Public Security Bureau Director discovered that the passport's seal was forged. The representative was summoned for interrogation and confessed to forging the document and falsely claiming to represent famine victims. He was arrested and transferred to the court for prosecution.

Provincial Committee Expedites Payment of Delinquent Deed Taxes: The Jiangsu Finance Department, concerned about the substantial arrears in deed taxes from various counties, dispatched Committee Member Tong Di-gu to Jiangdu, Yizheng, Taixian, Dongtai, Yancheng, Funing, and other counties to personally urge payment. Due to his inability to be present in this county, Zhang Cheng was specially assigned to investigate and expedite payment. A letter was sent to Finance Bureau Director Yu, urging him to submit a detailed table of all deed tax collections up to May of this year and to clear the accounts. Any allocated funds should be verified and jointly reported to facilitate the process.

Postponement of Datang Town Regular Route Launch: The Datang Inland Water Small Steamboat Company, since its establishment over thirty years ago, had an agreement with other inland water steamboat companies that Datang would not operate regular town clearing routes, and other small steamboats would not operate Yangzhou through routes. However, the Litong Company and others broke this agreement by operating Zhenjiang Taizhou routes, leading the Datang Company to also operate Zhenjiang through routes. The initial plan was to start on June 15th. It is now reported that, for the convenience of passengers, all wharves north of Yangzhou will remain the same. However, the wharves to the south require reinforced construction, and the Da Yang, Da Xiang, and other steamboats must undergo inspection procedures at Zhenjiang Customs, which have not yet been completed. Therefore, the launch, previously scheduled for June 15th, will be postponed.

The Truth About the Kidnapping for Ransom Case: A young woman surnamed Wang from a wealthy family in the northern countryside of Ganquan Mountain, Yangzhou, was kidnapped for ransom. Local officials dispatched detectives to apprehend Li Ma Si Zi, one of the perpetrators. It has been confirmed through interrogation that he has been detained. Seven other fugitives, including Li Wang and Chen, remain at large. It is also reported that the true nature of this case is a forced marriage rather than a kidnapping for ransom.

Report on the Jiwei Corps' Robbery and Extortion: The Taicheng Coastal Business reported that the Zidian shop in Huangqiao Town, Taiyu County, was robbed by the Jiwei Corps of the local area. They seized hundreds of yuan in cash and 120 packages of salt from the shop, and forced the shop assistants to sign a promissory note for 2,000 yuan, threatening violence if the money was not paid on time. Fearing for their lives due to such tyrannical behavior, they requested that the Transport Commissioner forward the report to the Salt Administration, requesting them to send troops to protect and investigate the matter.

Funing 79

Wujiaqiao Steamboat Robbery: A small steamboat on the Yancheng Funing route was returning to Yancheng from Funing yesterday afternoon (the 5th). About three hours into the journey, near Wujiaqiao, on the Yancheng border, dozens of bandits suddenly fired volley shots, damaging the steamboat's boiler. The bandits then jumped onto the boat and robbed the passengers of their silver, money, clothes, and jewelry. By the time the police team stationed at Goudun arrived, alerted by the report, the bandits had fled into the marshes.

Huzhou 80

Execution of Four Notorious Bandits: The Huzhou Bandit Suppression Command has captured forty to fifty bandits in the western countryside in recent days. Among them were Huang Tianba, a notorious bandit with a long record of crimes, Li San Mazi, a bandit from the Big Knife Society, and Ding Lao Er and Chuan Zu Xing, who were involved in harboring stolen goods. After interrogation by the military court, all the criminals confessed without hesitation. They have been detained for several days. This morning at ten o'clock, the Command brought Wang, Li, and the other two criminals to the South Training Ground in the city for execution by firing squad.

Ningbo 81

Maritime Police Bureau Dispatches Warships for Patrol: Yu Wenhan, Director of the Maritime Police Bureau, considering that the fishing season is commencing and fishermen are requesting protection, has specially dispatched Inspector Tang Lun to represent him on a patrol of the entire Zhejiang sea area to suppress maritime disturbances. It is reported that Mr. Tang departed from Zhenhai on the Haijing warship at 2 PM on the 10th.

Crackdown on Huahui Performers at Mount Dalan: The Intelligence Team Leader of the 6th Regiment of the Security Forces stationed at Mount Dalan received a secret report the day before yesterday that several Huahui performers were hiding in Li Jia Keng on Mount Dalan. Team Leader Chen, upon receiving the report, led soldiers to arrest them. The Huahui performers fled upon seeing the soldiers. Only Li Dehe, who owned the Huahui boat, was captured, and several Huahui scripts were seized. Team Leader Chen sent the captured individuals and evidence to the Baiguan Regiment Headquarters for interrogation. Yesterday morning, two soldiers were dispatched to escort them to the Ningbo Command for further processing.

Yinxian County Government Releases Idlers: The Yinxian County Government issued an order to the village and neighborhood committees yesterday, stating that, in accordance with the resolutions passed at the first administrative meeting regarding the implementation of releasing idlers and reforming funeral and wedding ceremonies, the county government will stipulate detailed measures. However, it is feared that long-standing habits are difficult to change, and the village and neighborhood committees may not be able to fully implement the plan. Therefore, the original measures have been slightly revised and are now promulgated for strict compliance. Two copies of the proclamation are to be posted.

Ministry of Education Promotes the National Phonetic Alphabet 83

After Wu Zhihui's methods for promoting the National Phonetic Alphabet were requested on the 11th of this month, the Ministry of Education held a discussion meeting of the National Phonetic Alphabet Promotion Committee at around 3:00 PM. Attendees included Wu Zhihui, Chen Jianxiao, Dai Yingguan, Huang Zunxian, Wang Rongchang, and Peng Baichuan. The items discussed and their results are as follows: 1. Notify Committee Members Liu Luyin, Zhao Yuanren, Lu Yiyan, and Zhang Shiyi that the meeting date will be postponed as Committee Member Wu Zhihui's draft of the National Phonetic Alphabet promotion methods has not yet been completed. 2. Before Committee Member Wu's draft is completed, Zhao Yuanren's Mandarin phonograph records and textbooks will be temporarily used for promotion. 3. Ministry of Education staff will begin learning the National Phonetic Alphabet starting next week, with the grouping method remaining the same as decided at the previous preparatory meeting. 4. Committee members will participate in the review of the training booklet this Friday. 5. The table of initials with voiced sounds proposed by Committee Member Wu will be printed and sent to the National Language Unification Preparatory Committee in Beijing and to all committee members for research. 6. The four tones (level, rising, departing, and entering) are limited to annotations on Chinese characters and not to the National Phonetic Alphabet. 7. The entering tone will be retained. 8. Training teachers is still necessary for researching the National Language and National Pronunciation, but it does not seem necessary for promoting the National Phonetic Alphabet.

The Ministry of Education staff's plan for learning the National Phonetic Alphabet was finalized on the 12th, dividing them into five groups: The Secretariat and the Counselor's Office, along with the Higher Education Department, will form one group, learning on Monday afternoons from 2:00 to 3:00 PM. The General Affairs Department has a larger number of staff and will be divided into two separate groups, learning on Tuesday and Wednesday mornings from 8:00 to 9:00 AM. The General Education Department, the Social Education Department, and the Mongolian-Tibetan Affairs Department will form one group, learning on Thursday mornings from 8:00 to 9:00 AM. The Compilation and Examination Department will be one group, learning on Friday mornings from 8:00 to 9:00 AM. The Promotion Committee will assign several individuals to preside over and convene the learning of each group on a daily basis.

Ministry of Education Cracks Down on Private Schools 84

The Ministry of Education has ordered all directly subordinate agencies to quickly report private secondary schools to the Ministry for record-keeping. The order states: "It has been repeatedly ordered that private secondary schools should submit applications for registration in accordance with the Regulations for Private Schools. Currently, the documents submitted by the various provincial and municipal education bureaus for the registration of private secondary schools either only list the school names without submitting other registration forms, or the Ministry orders supplementary reports after review, but they are delayed for a long time without reply. It seems that procedures are incomplete and cannot be considered formally registered. Graduates from these schools will not be accepted when public and private universities enroll new students in the 19th year, which is a very important matter. Each bureau should strictly comply with repeated orders to handle matters quickly to avoid mistakes." In addition to separate orders, a list of private secondary schools that have already been registered by the Ministry is issued for reference.

Local

Municipal Education Bureau 85

Deadline for Private Schools to Register

Submit Applications for Board of Directors Registration Before August of This Year

Chen Dezheng, Director of the Shanghai Special Municipal Education Bureau, believes that there are numerous private schools in the city, and many have not yet applied for registration. This not only makes supervision difficult but also often causes delays in students' studies. He has issued another strict order for all private primary and secondary schools in the city to apply for registration within a limited time. The order states: "It has been repeatedly ordered that all private primary and secondary schools in this city should submit applications for registration in accordance with the Regulations for Private Schools. Currently, although many private primary and secondary schools in this city have complied with the regulations and submitted applications for registration, there are still many who are waiting and seeing. Therefore, it is specially stipulated again that all private primary and secondary schools in this city that have not yet applied for registration must apply for registration before the end of August of this year. At the very least, they should apply for registration with the board of directors before August of this year. It is hereby urgently ordered that all primary and secondary schools in this city comply with this order."

Municipal Education Bureau Junior High School Joint Examination Discussion Meeting 86

The Municipal Education Bureau has prepared very meticulously for this junior high school graduation joint examination. On the 12th, they convened all junior high school graduation joint examination supervisors and graders in the bureau's conference room to discuss various supervision and grading issues. Those who attended included Section Chief Ni of the Municipal Education Bureau, Chuan Hou Tian, Li Dachao, Tang Shouqian, Zhang Duanzhen, Zhou Shang, Zhang Tianen, Dai Ying, Zhang Huibao, and other nine people. School representatives included Zi Rongguang and Zhu Mingxin from Chengli Middle School, Feng Zhengjun from Junyi Middle School, Zhou Yongnan and Zhou Puxian from Nanyang Middle School, Liu Shunzai from the Municipal Training Department, Li Chuanshu and Ge Xiaoyan from Nanyang Middle School, Hu Jingzhi and Ding Shaohuan from Pudong Middle School, Lu Zulong from Wusong Middle School, Yao Wenxun and Li Shandao from Zheng Yixin Guangzhao Middle School, Dai Yuheng and Wu Peiwei from Xue Shao Municipal North Middle School, Zhang Zhongyu and Yu Tianxi from Jianguo Middle School, Sun Zhenxian and Jiang Wenbao from Minli Middle School, Tu Shaokai and Yang Xibin from Zhang Xin Chang Minli Girls' Middle School, Kong Junyi and Zhang Weixin from Yuan An Jingye Middle School, Zhu Xianghu and Niu Changzai from Fudan Affiliated Middle School, Xu Zongze and Bao Huai from Bai Yang Zu Zhang Wuben Girls' Middle School, Wu Jingzhi and Rong Fangzhou from Chen Dingxiu Shanghai University Affiliated Middle School, Shao Hongzhi and Duan Rende from Song Wenhan Daxia Middle School, Zeng Guangdian and Liu Yiqing from Wu Weicheng Zhongxi Girls' Middle School, Li Zhenggan and Zhu Lanzhen from Lu Guiliang, etc. (1) The meeting began with formalities. (2) Chairman Wang Ni Kechang Wen Ya recorded Zhang Huibao. (3) The chairman reported briefly that this bureau's joint examination has a total of 1,800 students from 67 schools, with approximately 15,000 test papers in seven subjects as of today. Assistance from the various schools is required regarding the supervision and grading of the examination. It is deeply appreciated that everyone has been able to attend during this busy period. In view of the complex educational situation in this city and the varying levels of each school, even just considering the textbooks used by each school, which this bureau recently sent personnel to investigate, there are already more than 300 types. It is conceivable that the joint examination was decided to investigate the achievements of each school and increase educational efficiency. However, as this is a new undertaking, although preparations have been mostly completed, it is still feared that there may be shortcomings. It is hoped that everyone will express their opinions and discuss together. Then, printed materials such as the "Examination Supervisor and Grader Guidelines," "Examination Rules for Examinees," and "Examination Scoring Methods" were distributed. Director Ni then explained each item one by one, and everyone was satisfied. (4) Distribute supervisor badges. (5) Representatives from various schools expressed their opinions separately: A. Guangzhao suggested whether there were standards for grading test papers. B. Zhongxi suggested that, as this is the first joint examination in this city, and due to the special circumstances of each school, it is proposed that the graders be more lenient when grading the test papers. Two Zhongxi suggested whether the supervisors could change the route due to the long distance. C. Fudan Affiliated Middle School requested that the bureau provide answer keys for each subject to facilitate the graders' assessment. D. Fudan Affiliated Middle School requested that the bureau organize a middle school curriculum standard research committee to announce the curriculum and order each school to follow and standardize the level. E. Guangzhao requested that the bureau designate two subject grading supervisors to discuss the grading standards with each representative and determine the detailed rules for grading that subject together. (6) Director Ni answered each of the above questions one by one as follows: (A) Each subject's exam is based on testing, but test questions are still used to divide the grading fairly, hoping to avoid excessive subjectivity. Fortunately, the questions were extremely carefully prepared beforehand. (B) The varying levels of each school were originally a fact, as mentioned earlier. The results of the investigation of textbooks used by each school showed that there were no fewer than 300 types. As for the exam questions, they are based on the middle school curriculum standards promulgated by the Ministry of Education, using the minimum standard for junior high school graduates in each subject. However, I believe that although it is not overly strict, it will definitely not result in everyone graduating, which would be equivalent to not taking the exam. (C) The supervisors should contact each other and make adjustments, but the bureau must be notified. (D) The bureau has already prepared the answer keys for each subject. (E) The bureau hired experts last year to organize a middle school curriculum standard research committee and ordered each school to conduct a trial of the additions and deletions. (F) A detailed discussion will be held in groups on the afternoon of the 19th. (7) The case of grading papers by representatives of various schools was resolved by the representatives of each school recognizing each other on the spot. (8) The meeting adjourned.

Junior High School Joint Examination Supervisor Guidelines 87

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau has formulated the following Junior High School Joint Examination Supervisor and Grader Guidelines: (1) The examination dates are from June 16th to 19th. (2) Arrive at the examination location before 8:00 AM each day. (3) The examination papers will be sent directly to the examination location by the bureau. (4) The examination will start on time at 8:30 AM and the examination papers will be distributed. (5) The examination will stop on time at 11:30 AM and 4:30 PM and the examination papers will be collected. (6) Check the examinee's photos at any time. (7) The examinee's photos should be submitted to the bureau supervisor after collection. (8) After the completion of each subject's examination, the examination papers will be taken back by the bureau supervisor and grader. (9) Do not leave the examination site during supervision except in special circumstances. (10) Pay attention to the examination rules for graduates and enforce them strictly. (11) Lunch will be provided at the examination location each day. (12) The period for grading the examination papers is from 2:00 PM on June 19th to 12:00 AM on June 22nd. (13) Arrive at the bureau at Daji Road, New West Gate, at 8:00 AM each day to grade the examination papers together. (14) Meals will be provided at the bureau during the grading period. (15) Grading will be divided into groups by examination subject. (16) The number of graders for each subject is tentatively set at eight. (17) Each student's overall score will be calculated by averaging the scores of each grader. (18) The examination papers for each subject at each examination site should be compiled separately. (19) The examination papers should be sealed and signed by the supervisor after the examination papers are collected, and the number of examination papers should be indicated. (20) The school负责人 should sign in with the supervisor before leading the students to the examination site. Shanghai Citizens' Federation

Declaration on Recovering Educational Rights in Concessions 88

The preparatory committee of the Shanghai Citizens' Federation issued a declaration yesterday on recovering educational rights in concessions, saying: "For decades, we have paid little attention to the educational administration within the Shanghai concessions. As a result, foreigners have taken over and replaced it. When foreigners took over, we were still unaware of the loss of educational rights. Only today, under the blue sky and white sun and the Kuomintang's reforms, do we realize the loss of educational administrative power. Therefore, we are urgently seeking to recover it. However, at this time of economic hardship, creating a large number of schools and concentrating students is not something that can be achieved with simple words. If we can have appropriate planning for the educational finances in the concessions, as the central government and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs have said, if our country can increase the number of schools so that all Chinese children can study at home, then educational rights will have been recovered invisibly. We recognize that this is difficult to achieve at this time. However, looking at the current situation, we should first order the schools run by foreigners to add courses on party doctrine, and we should increase the allocation of educational funds within the concessions to enhance the rights and interests and improve the progress of education. This is one point. Chinese should be hired to manage the educational administration and affairs within the concessions to achieve consistency in education. This is the second point. The above two points are the necessary methods for resolving the issue of educational rights in the concessions today. It is the urgent task for those of us who advocate recovering educational rights in the concessions. In addition to expressing our support and contributing our opinions to the municipal government, this federation hereby declares that we hope that all Chinese citizens in the concessions will work together to promote the practical benefits for the future of education."

Japanese referees' perspective on

Far East Three Nations Basketball 94

Self-Admiration (Zeng Yanhua)

The details of unfair refereeing in the 9th Far East Games basketball matches have been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. This is especially true for basketball, where players from the Chinese and Philippine teams have to endure the situation in each game, which is extremely sad and tragic. Even Japanese spectators with some sense of judgment are roaring in disapproval. Experts in the newspapers also criticize the referees for their mistakes. All of this is enough to prove that justice prevails. Who would have thought that referee Tanaka Kanjiro would dare to write a lengthy article with a large headline, using sophistry to refute everything? After reading it, I couldn't help but laugh. Therefore, I have translated the original text in detail for relevant parties and sports enthusiasts to read.

"I (Tanaka referring to himself), as a basketball referee of the Far East Games, feel it may be inappropriate to offer unreserved criticism of the three national teams from a referee's perspective. However, I cannot ignore etiquette because my attitude as a referee has been misunderstood by the general public. This kind of slander may be due to the audience not fully understanding the rules or because the intense emotions of the game have led to misinterpretations. I could have dismissed it, but I cannot remain silent about the fact that the refereeing is unfair. I fear that the misunderstanding of the attitude of referees will spread and not only damage the authority of referees but also tarnish the reputation of the Japanese basketball community."

"We should have noble character, and so should the teams. The main elements of a team's character are fairness, uprightness, and sportsmanship. Fewer fouls are a manifestation of fairness and uprightness. Some actions, while not constituting fouls, may still violate sportsmanship during the game. Regardless of the outcome, if I were to discuss the character of each team, I would say that Japan is the best because their performance avoids physical contact, thus reducing fouls. This is not to say that the Japanese team never commits fouls. For example, Kobayashi, a key defender, also committed four fouls. However, the fouls he committed were generally unavoidable. Although he tried his best, his body movements were clumsy, or he misjudged the opponent's actions, resulting in unintentional fouls."

"Next is the Chinese team. Although they committed many fouls, they were all simple mistakes. It is clear that there was no malicious intent. This may be due to the Chinese team's relaxed approach compared to the Japanese team, or because the level of refereeing and understanding of the rules varied, making the players unaccustomed. However, during the second game between China and Japan, the attitude and actions of the Chinese players towards the referee seemed to be somewhat misunderstood. Despite this minor flaw, I still believe that the Chinese team is second best because of their pure temperament and emotions. The Philippine team uses tricks to deceive the referee. If we were to consider seniority, the Philippine team would be the best among the three. Therefore, their fouls are also very clever, using all kinds of tricks to deceive the audience and lure ignorant people to sympathize with them, trying to shift the blame onto the referee and the opponent's actions. Therefore, it is common to hear foul language during the game, which is very unfortunate and regrettable. (Translator's note: There are more than a thousand words criticizing the behavior of the Philippine team's players, which is exceptionally blunt. Because there are many words and mistakes, I have omitted them.)

"I am often shocked by the many violations committed by the Chinese and Philippine teams, especially the fouls of dribbling the ball while running and double dribbling, which occur frequently. The Chinese team's center often jumps and taps the ball before the referee throws it to the highest point. The Philippine team also often violates this rule. It seems that the two teams lack a full understanding of the new jump ball rules implemented this year, especially the Philippine team, which seems to be completely unaware of it and violates it frequently. During jump balls, the Chinese team's center often commits charging fouls, raising his left hand to the opponent's chest to prevent him from jumping or jumping diagonally in front of him, repeatedly committing fouls for unknown reasons. The Philippine players are even more likely to commit fouls of dribbling the ball while running more than dribbling the ball. The next is double dribbling. This kind of violation really kills the true value of the players' skills. Charging fouls and other violations are sometimes unavoidable, but double dribbling is not. If the players can use a little reason, they can absolutely avoid it. The fact that the Chinese and Philippine teams commit this violation a lot seems to prove that their performance is not fully practiced and proficient. The Japanese players do not commit these violations and charging fouls because they are accustomed to strict refereeing and coaches teaching the rules every night."

"In summary, although I do not have an exact memory, the number of fouls committed by the Chinese and Philippine teams must be several times higher than that of Japan. Those who criticize the referee's handling by simply comparing the number of fouls are ignorant of the referee's duties. Why do the Chinese and Philippine teams commit so many fouls? A well-intentioned explanation may be attributed to the negligence of domestic referees in China and the Philippines, resulting in bad habits becoming natural. Whenever the expedition team questioned the judgment, I tried my best to explain it earnestly. If I saw something inappropriate, I would also offer an explanation. If there was a suitable opportunity, I would not hesitate to give hints and reminders. I asked myself if my attitude was unnecessary. Therefore, the kindness I showed to the expedition team must have been considerably unfavorable to Japan. However, I intended to actively seek to eliminate the disadvantages of the expedition within the rules. I believe that the Chinese and Philippine teams will definitely understand my painstaking efforts." "I, as a referee for this Far East basketball tournament, have been deeply impressed by the admirable character of the Chinese team captain, Li Guochen. He has sufficient qualifications and immediately suppresses his violent behavior when he sees the feelings of his teammates. His calm attitude is admirable. The forward, Tang Baokun, has no complaints or dissatisfaction with the referee's decisions. These two gentlemen are the most well-trained and have a noble character, which Japanese players should emulate. The Philippine team coach, Huela Neiva, is also a good coach. He often comes to shake hands and praise my fair refereeing after the game, adding many words of encouragement. During the Japan-Philippines game, he worked hard to suppress the dissatisfaction of the supporters, which is very gratifying. I would like to express my full respect for the sportsmanship of all the aforementioned gentlemen and use it to conclude this article."

Feelings After Translation: Mr. Tanaka never penalized the Japanese players for violating sportsmanship during the game. He severely criticized the Philippine players for their tricks, but he may not know that the Japanese players also took advantage of the referee's protection and secretly used insidious tactics everywhere. As for dribbling the ball while running, the Japanese players committed the most fouls, but he turned a blind eye. When the ball was thrown into the circle, it was always biased towards the Japanese side. Three people surrounded one person, and two people sandwiched one person, but he did not call a foul. Instead, he shouted for a jump ball. In short, his reverse explanation showed that he had lost the authority of the referee. His clumsy expression was almost the object of ridicule on the field. In the final section, he falsely claimed that the Philippine team's coach praised his fairness. I still remember that before the last minute of the championship final, a reporter ran to the Philippine team's players' seat to wait for the captain to talk. After the game, coach Hui ran onto the field, his face stern, and scolded Tanaka, saying, "My team is not only fighting five people but also dealing with seven people and still able to win. What else do you have to say?" These few words not only made Tanaka lose face but also made the Japanese spectators look at each other in silence. The clumsiness of other refereeing skills was never seen before. It is not enough to criticize his incompetence. In short, he, as a referee, had absolutely no experience in major international competitions, leading to this embarrassment and leaving a fragrant name in the history of the Far East Games basketball tournament. I deeply regret it and sigh.

Winning the World Heavyweight Boxing Championship

Mark Schmeling 95

丨German Mark Defeats American Sharkey

Surrounded by opponents, Sharkey had the advantage. As a result, he failed due to an illegal cold punch. The world heavyweight boxing match, a scene of dragon and tiger fighting, was held yesterday in New York's Yankee Stadium. German Mark恭墨林 won the championship. The victory was not due to his strength conquering his opponent, American Jack Sharkey, but because Sharkey violated the rules and was declared defeated by the referee.

Sharkey's Unearned Gain 96

In the first four rounds of the battle between the two heroes, Sharkey had a clear advantage. The first, third, and fourth rounds can be said to be the autumn of Sharkey's power surge. Only the third round was the heyday of Schmeling. Judging from the overall situation, eight or nine out of ten of this championship would go to Sharkey. Unexpectedly, when the bell rang to signal the end of the fourth round, Sharkey suddenly delivered a cold punch. Schmeling fell to the corner of the ring, shouting that he had been tricked. The referee, with a clear eye, resolutely declared Sharkey's violation. The title of chief champion was awarded to Schmeling. Losing a horse may not be a blessing. The outcome was not what Sharkey had initially expected.

Schmeling, the German Who Won the World Heavyweight Boxing Championship 97

The Audience Expresses Discontent 98

Every year, when the world heavyweight boxing championship is held, the whole country is crazy. This is because Americans usually love this sport like their lives. Now that two famous American and German players have met, it is appropriate that the place is crowded with people. There were 75,000 spectators in total, of which three-fifths were leaning towards Sharkey. Even Thornton, the former champion who has retired, said that Schmeling lacks experience and agility, not as sure as Sharkey. After four rounds, Sharkey's efforts to fight were deeply praised by the audience. However, the general public believes that the illegal action recognized by the referee was because Sharkey's punch coincided with the bell. Therefore, the crowd was excited and uproar, but the referee's order was like a mountain and could not be changed.

The Social Bureau Temporarily Approves the Highest

White Japonica Rice Price Increase of One Yuan 100

The Whole Country is Almost in a State of Food Shortage

Reduce the Waste of Polishing Brown Rice

The Municipal Social Bureau, in view of the recent rice market being scarce, convened representatives of various rice industry groups on the 9th of this month to discuss maintaining the food supply in the city. After three hours of discussion, it was temporarily decided to increase the maximum price of white japonica rice by one yuan, totaling twenty-one yuan, while strictly prohibiting hidden price cuts. After receiving the report, the Social Bureau still believes that the rice price should not remain high for a long time. Considering the three aspects of food, hygiene, and business difficulties, it is only limiting the degree of brown rice polishing. The original order stated that in order to comply with the matter, this bureau convened representatives of the industry groups to the bureau on the 9th of this month to discuss maintaining the city's food supply. According to reports, the representatives of the groups who attended the meeting on that day stated that the production cost was high and the time was approaching the harvest, making it difficult to maintain the original price limit. After detailed discussion, the whole group decided to increase the maximum rice price by one yuan, totaling twenty-one yuan, while strictly prohibiting hidden price cuts. Those who violate the rules will be severely punished. The representatives of the industry groups were indeed sincere, but they still followed the trend of the Shanghai market. The public associations can take the food of the people as important and make it level. Moreover, the time for new production is still far away, and the price increase is not appropriate. Considering that the representatives can be responsible for implementation and will no longer break the rules, if there is any hidden price cut, they are willing to accept severe punishment. Since it has been decided and reported, it is temporarily approved. However, the limited highest white rice is nothing more than its fine polishing, which is commonly known as special machine japonica rice. Each stone of brown rice can only produce seven斗 of polished rice. The bran produced in the last time is as white as powder. The kind of rice quality has lost its nutrients as verified by the bureau. Eating it will turn into beriberi, heart and other diseases. The citizens are accustomed to the old habits of eating this high-priced and useless rice because they do not know its disadvantages. They only greed for the convenience of smooth swallowing. At this time, the food shortage is almost in the whole country, so it is all dependent on foreign rice to supply, and they still eat this fine white high-priced rice. It is a waste of natural resources and damages the people's food. For the sake of the people's food, for the sake of the people's hygiene, there is an urgent need to reform. It is proposed that the loss of brown japonica rice should not be less than 7.5, and only be higher than 8.5. That is, each stone of brown japonica rice produces more than one斗 of white rice than before. Ten stones will produce one stone more, which is enough for a family of eight for a month. Moreover, the rice price is reduced by the decrease in waste, and the current price per stone can also be reduced by one or two yuan. In this way, it takes into account the people's food and business feelings, and there is no omission. Therefore, the order is given to the public association to immediately notify the industry merchants to comply with it within a short period of time. After this period, the rice price will be uniformly reduced to below 20 yuan. Do not violate this order.

The Business Consolidation Association Announces

Relief Fund Price Increase Measures 101

Fully Promote Domestic Products to Reduce Imports

Suppress the Rebellion and Pacify the Bandits to Increase Production of Goods

Limit Margin and Futures Trading to Purchase Exchange Bills

Import and Export Industries Settle Prices at Any Time to Avoid Danger

The Business Consolidation Association officially announced four measures for the relief fund price increase yesterday. They are recorded as follows:

Since the price of gold in the world market has gradually risen, our country is using silver standard, which is appropriate to its impact. Those who are engaged in import and export trade are daily affected by the instability of the exchange rate, and the collapse of the connection occurs from time to time. Its operation is no less than rolling into the tide. From the consumer's point of view, the number of clothing, food and daily necessities required for foreign countries has increased due to the rapid increase in commodity prices, and the standard of living has invisibly increased. Therefore, the gold price problem is not only the partial interest relationship of importers and exporters, but the interest relationship of the whole people. Since this issue has occurred, the association has received letters from various groups requesting a proper remedy for the authorities to adopt and to express the suffering of the business community. The association believes that the two ministers of finance and industry of one party attach great importance to this issue. The master plan has been seen in the newspapers, and they are both important officials in charge of the country's industry and finance. When sitting and talking, there should be people who can meet the expectations of the people. On the one hand, economic experts often contribute their research to the people of the country, and most of them hold an unbreakable economic theory and social phenomenon. Since they are self-respecting, they are more afraid that the sacrifice of the humble will turn into a mountain of damage. They have repeatedly consulted with the financial community and various groups, and all think that among the suggestions from all parties, such as prohibiting margin trading and taxing silver bars, the effect may be temporarily to make the gold and silver exchange rates change slightly, but this kind of artificial suppression method will eventually not be able to thoroughly reverse the echo or come out of our intentions. And considering that this remedy is related to various problems in the world economy and our country's political and social problems, there may be a claim to implement the gold standard or order the exchange rate standard. Because our country's currency has not yet been unified and there is no preparation at present, it cannot be achieved in one fell swoop. Moreover, politicians and economists have been exploring for several months and have not been able to find a concrete plan for implementation, which shows that fundamental relief is not easy. Even the palliative method must be carefully considered. The association's research has found that the comparative harm is less or can be a remedy for the present. There are about four measures, which are described as follows for the criticism of the people of the country. Our country's import exceeds its difference, and the opening system that has increased over the years, so the more the gold price rises, the more unfavorable the exchange rate is, and the greater the debt of international payments. To reduce this kind of damage, the method is only to start from reversing the import surplus of trade (1) Actively promote domestic products to replace imported goods to reduce imports. The four words of promoting domestic products have long become common terms in society, but the publicity has been long and there is no significant effect. It is not just that the parties only know to promote but cannot implement. The fact is that they are also blamed. Some only care about the partial interests and fail to use the general strength to promote them all. Therefore, the slogans have been years, and the results are still not fresh. For example, the cigarette industry promotes domestic cigarettes and restricts the affiliated companies to strictly abide by them, but other domestic products have no direct interest relationship with themselves, or even put them on hold. Secondly, party and government personnel have the obligation to set an example, and the government has repeatedly ordered and declared, but the facts and the documents may not be consistent. If the three circles of the party, the people, and the business community are still like this, then the remaining consumers will only seek the convenience of purchasing and use, and what more time to carefully identify them. Therefore, the promotion of domestic products in the future should concentrate the strength of the entire society and unite. The method should be that the chambers of commerce in various places organize special committees to promote domestic products to take responsibility for investigation, research and propaganda. On the one hand, the universal establishment of domestic products cooperatives provides people with the convenience of selecting and purchasing domestic products anytime and anywhere (2) Increase the production of products to increase the number of exports. Those who export raw materials from our country to foreign countries often think that the import surplus of international trade and the backwardness of industry are important reasons for this. However, since our country has been in war and banditry for years and there have been strange disasters in the northwest, agricultural products have changed from a large export to a large import, such as foreign rice and flour, which have been increasing year by year. To reverse this trade trend and make the export gradually smooth, it is thought that now when the government is revising the export tariff, it is only necessary to select the large exports of our country, which have a long history and have been imitated by various countries, and are gradually retreating in the position of being unable to compete, or these exports are currently young and will have the hope of development in the future, all of which are exempt from export tariffs to provide assistance. On the one hand, we actively suppress chaos and eliminate bandits so that traffic will not be congested, and farmers have arable land, and merchants can transport goods, so that international trade will gradually balance, and the damage caused by the gold and silver parity exchange rate can be reduced (3) Restrict non-importers and exporters from trading margin and futures or purchasing foreign exchange bills. Bank foreign exchange is also limited to import and export transactions. When people discuss the skyrocketing of gold prices, they often think that it is caused by speculation and manipulation, so there is a proposal to temporarily suspend the trading of gold exchanges. According to the facts, futures trading itself has the effect of leveling commodity prices, so it is not easy to punish all of them for fear of speculators' manipulation. The fact that it is not a business need but only to win unexpected profits is a significant fact. Adding restrictions will not hinder the unexpected wealth, and or it is enough to reduce the chaos in the market (4) Those who are engaged in import and export industries should settle prices at any time to avoid the danger of bearing the rise and fall of gold and silver parity in the future. The current damage to the foreign goods industry caused by the rising gold price is, in a nutshell, that the price was not settled when the contract was concluded, which led to the fact that the goods expected when the previous order was not enough. It is even more than double the original amount. If the goods are not issued after the order arrives in Shanghai, they will be sued by foreign merchants. If the goods are issued, the sales of the customer help are blocked, and the goods are difficult to sell. It is difficult to remove the goods due to the capital limit. During the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, Shanghai's cotton and wool had already experienced this panic once. However, the current rise in the price of gold is still endless, which is even more fierce and unpredictable than the situation after the European war. At that time, some people who settled the price in advance were not affected by this unexpected loss. There is a saying, "If you do not forget the past, you can be a teacher of the future." It is true that the proportion of the quantity of orders placed by our country's merchants engaged in import and export and the capital they have prepared is often very different, so most of them are unwilling to settle the price when the order is placed, so that the operating funds are not easy to circulate. However, in view of the dangerous advantages and disadvantages of the skyrocketing and falling of gold and silver, it is appropriate to gradually think about changing the plan in order to tend to a stable one. Even for capital reasons, the order can be settled first, and the price of the goods can be paid off when the goods arrive, which can be carried out simultaneously and without using the settlement of the price and the payment of the settlement as a talk. The danger of gold and silver rising and falling is turned to the daily.

In addition to the second item, which must be presided over by the government before it can be implemented, the remaining three items are deemed to be practical and have no obstacles, and after implementation, there may be considerable effects, then all those in the business community are responsible for rising up and implementing them. It is hoped that they will not hesitate to consider and correct them.

Zhang Jingjiang's Talk 102

Denies Advocating Peace Movement

Zhang Jingjiang, Chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, came to Shanghai from Beijing the night before last after finishing his official duties. The reporters of various newspapers made a special trip to Zhang's residence at 98 Massenet Road to pay their respects. When they were greeted, the reporters asked if there was anything wrong with the report that Mr. Zhang telegraphed to advocate peace. Zhang replied that last time I went to Xuzhou, a certain newspaper fabricated a peace telegram. At that time, I telegraphed to the mayor of Shanghai, Zhang, and asked him to investigate and publish it in various newspapers. Yesterday, a certain newspaper reported that Commander-in-Chief Chiang suddenly returned to Beijing by plane, and Mr. Zhang went to the headquarters to discuss peace methods. I think it is also a deliberate rumor. I often travel between Beijing, Shanghai and Hangzhou because the Construction Committee and Zhejiang Province have something to discuss and contact. My actions have no value to pay attention to. I arrived in Beijing the day before yesterday and returned last night and have not been to the headquarters. Chairman Chiang has not returned to Beijing either. This kind of fabrication is completely from the hands of imperialists and reactionary elements, so as to confuse the audience. It is not worth the knowledge of the wise. It is a pity that some newspapers that do not distinguish between the truth and falsehood of the facts rashly disclose it, which is not only devoid of common sense of news, but also undermines the reputation of their newspapers. Ask Mr. Zhang if he will return to Hangzhou soon or still have to go to Beijing? I will go to Hangzhou tomorrow to take care of official affairs. The reporter asked to leave immediately and left.

The Ministry of Industry and Commerce previously convened representatives from Shanghai's industrial and commercial sectors to elect members to prepare for the organization of the Industrial and Commercial Management Association. Promote Domestic Goods Association

Convening a General Meeting of Factory Representatives 113

Regarding participation in the Qingdao Municipal National Products Exhibition
