National Products Bank

Issuing Wages on Behalf of the Dredging Bureau 114

Notice of Important Matters

Director Song of the Dredging Bureau, in view of the major robbery and injury case that occurred on the 30th of last month, in order to reduce the danger, discussed with the directors and chief engineers to entrust the National Products Bank to issue wages on his behalf. Yesterday, a special notice was issued stating that the salary capital for the construction and dredging sections of the bureau this month will be issued at the National Products Bank on Hankou Road, Shanghai. All the following matters should be noted: "Time": From 10:00 AM to 8:00 PM on Sunday, the 29th of this month. "Travel": For personnel from Zhang Huabang, the bureau will separately provide the third-class train fare. For personnel from Zhoujiazui, the bureau will separately provide the third-class tram fare. For personnel on various ships, the bureau's tugboat will pick them up. "Procedures": Each person must personally go to the bank to collect their salary and be given a passbook with a small photo of themselves attached (people will be sent by the bureau to take photos at various locations) and their signature or fingerprint. One yuan in foreign currency must be deposited in each passbook when opening the passbook and cannot be withdrawn. After receiving the passbook, it must be carefully kept for future use. If you wish to open a savings account at the bank, you can contact the bank yourself. "Shifts": Personnel from each work site and ship must be evenly divided into two shifts and go to the bank to collect their salaries on the dates listed above. Each time, the number of people leaving their posts cannot exceed half of the total number. During this time, the ship owners or foremen must be especially careful in their duties to ensure the safety of the ships. On the second day, all personnel must start work as usual without delay. Dredging Bureau, June 11, 19th year.

Recent News from the Maritime Industry 115

Collision between Two Ships: The European ship "Atreus Maru" of the Japanese Osaka Company was loading cargo in Shanghai for London. As it was casting off near the 13th buoy in the Huangpu River, the "Dakichi Maru" of the Japanese Nisshin Company, which was carrying cargo for export in Shanghai, was sailing to that spot. Due to the rapid current in the river, the ship could not go straight and was hit by the current. It crashed into the outer hull of the "Atreus Maru", damaging the steel plate of the ship's hull. The cargo was not damaged. The hull of the "Dakichi Maru" was also slightly damaged, but it was not serious, so it continued to export as usual. The Osaka Company immediately reported the damage to the customs surveyor, and then repaired it itself while negotiating with Nisshin for compensation. It is now heard that the "Atreus Maru" has been repaired and will set sail immediately, and Nisshin has agreed to pay the repair costs.

Yichang Ship Repair: The American Jitjiang Company specializes in the Yangtze River route. The Yichang, its direct ship from Shanghai to Chongqing, was originally scheduled to load cargo in Shanghai for Chongqing today. Yesterday, because the ship's machinery was slightly damaged, the customs announced that it would be postponed for two days to facilitate repairs. Therefore, yesterday, the company had notified each passenger that the Yichang ship would be changed to leave Shanghai on Monday.

Osaka Merchant Shipping's Six New Ships Sailing to America 116

The first ship will sail on July 5th.

In order to compete in the Shanghai-New York route, Osaka Merchant Shipping Co. commissioned six motor-powered ships from the Nagasaki Mitsubishi Shipyard. This matter has been reported in this newspaper. The first ship, Kinai Maru, weighing 10,000 tons, was launched in April and completed on June 2nd. The test run showed that it can travel 18 nautical miles per hour. The hull is entirely made of steel, so it is extremely strong and has a very high speed. From Shanghai to New York via Los Angeles in the Pacific Ocean and through the Panama Canal, it only takes 38 days to arrive. This ship will depart from Shanghai on July 5th for its maiden voyage to New York. There are also five ships, Tokai Maru, Sanyo Maru, Hokuyo Maru, Kanto Maru, and Kansai Maru, which are arranged in the same way as the Kinai Maru, with beautiful decorations and extremely high speed. The interior of the ships is divided into cabins for gold, silver, valuable cargo, Huzhou silk, tung oil, etc., all of which are the latest construction. These five ships can also come to Shanghai for operation before the end of the year.

Miao Zhongxiu Discusses the Recent Situation of Raw Silk Inspection 118

Since the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau's Raw Silk Inspection Office implemented various inspections, silk merchants have been spared unnecessary losses and are quite satisfied. Inspection certificates have also gradually gained the trust of foreign countries. However, some silk merchants have failed to understand the true meaning of various inspections, saying that uniform inspection processes silk factories or that public measurement inspection reduces the amount are all misunderstandings. According to Miao Zhongxiu, director of the department, uniform inspection is especially important in raw silk quality inspection. The United States pays the most attention to it, and France has also gradually increased its attention. The inspection in this office maintains the fairness of trade between buyers and sellers, and the so-called inspection of raw silk depends on its quality and the score determined by it. There is no distinction between leniency and strictness. Those with poor quality will naturally fail the inspection, while those with excellent quality will naturally pass the inspection. Recently, some silk factories have even been given price increases after inspection because of their excellent quality exceeding the specified inspection standards, which proves that the claim that uniform inspection is too strict is actually unfounded. As for public measurement inspection, the results are different due to changes in climate and the amount of water content. Recently, due to the dry climate, the number of public measurements exceeding the net measurements has been the highest, while the number of net measurements exceeding the public measurements has gradually decreased. In short, the main purpose of the government's implementation of inspection is to completely maintain the fairness of trade and prevent any party from suffering undue losses.

Citywide

Open Letter to Compatriots from Cotton Textile Workers 121

The cotton textile workers of Shanghai issued an open letter to compatriots yesterday, saying that since the industrial revolution, capitalist countries have naturally and absolutely formed two phenomena in production: (1) overproduction; (2) lack of raw materials. In order to solve these two phenomena, they must find colonies to sell their surplus products and find ways to seize agricultural products from colonies to supply their raw materials. Many places in the world are used by capitalist countries to sell surplus products and seize raw materials, especially our China. Mr. Sun Yat-sen has already said that our country is simply a semi-colony that is worse than a colony, which is not wrong at all. After the Opium War, international imperialism used force to oppress us and set various unequal treaties that bound us, making our industry unable to develop forever and becoming a place for their economic aggression for a long time. The inability to control tariffs is a great example. For more than 80 years, our industry has not been able to develop at all, resulting in factory closures and worker unemployment, which is so painful. People's lives are nothing more than clothing, food, housing, and transportation, and clothing is especially important. In China, where industry is backward and people's lives are declining, the purchasing power of ordinary people is very low. Therefore, the importance of cotton textiles is even more obvious. Because cotton textiles have become indispensable to ordinary civilians, and the value is cheap and the material is durable, various domestic industries are doing their best to promote them. However, in the end, because the unequal treaties have not been abolished and tariffs cannot be controlled, foreign countries still have the opportunity to compete. With unequal treaties as a protective talisman, they tax their goods very lightly, thus reducing prices and using the psychology of people being greedy for cheap things to fulfill their desire to suppress the development of domestic industry. May I ask how can the cotton textile industry, which is in its infancy with short capital and lack of experience in our country, not plummet? Our country's request for the prosperity of the cotton textile industry to save the decline of China's industry is undoubtedly to abolish the unequal treaties and promote domestic goods. This is what our party, government, and people of China are working together and advocating day and night. This is also the only way we cotton textile workers believe to solve this problem. We always firmly believe that to save China's overall crisis today, there is no other way but to fight under the leadership of the Chinese Kuomintang based on the Three People's Principles. However, there are still many people who take advantage of the various topics of China's industrial downturn to oppress or exploit the interests of workers. Taking our cotton textile workers in Shanghai as an example, when the cotton textile industry was developed, there were more than 4,000 organized members. Now, due to unemployment, it has been reduced to more than 1,900, of which more than 2,000 are unemployed. The party and government are naturally eager to remedy the situation, but the capitalists often do not follow the guidance and orders of the party and government agencies. The lives of cotton textile workers are lower and more painful than those of any other workers. On the contrary, the working hours are more than 10 hours a day. How can this kind of hard and low-paid life of cattle and horses be in line with the purpose of Mr. Sun Yat-sen's policy for workers? Now, the cost of living in Shanghai is increasing day by day. The wages earned by the workers cannot only not supply themselves and support their parents, wives, and children at home, but they also have to receive the terrible news of factory closures from time to time. We know that to save the decline of China's cotton industry, on the positive side, we can only strive to abolish the unequal treaties under the leadership of the party. On the negative side, in addition to requesting the party and government to prevent those who do not understand what Mr. Sun Yat-sen said, "Reducing working hours, increasing worker protection fees, and increasing productivity instead," from destroying our workers by taking advantage of the various topics of industrial downturn, we can only ask compatriots from all walks of life to give us considerable assistance. From the anti-Japanese movement in the past, "Stopping enemy goods is enough to put the imperialists to death." To save the decline of the cotton textile industry, before the unequal treaties are abolished, we can only ask compatriots from all walks of life to endure the loss of domestic goods being cheaper than foreign goods, and not hesitate to support the prosperity of the national industry, to remedy the decline of the cotton textile industry, and to relieve the lives of cotton textile workers across the country, and sacrifice a small amount of money and strive to promote domestic goods to resist foreign goods. It is not only the dying cotton textile workers who are telling the truth, but also fulfilling the responsibility of a citizen. Compatriots, this is a big concern for the survival of our entire China. Work hard and strive to make a final struggle for the country! Our city's cotton textile workers, at the time of imminent death, call for the realization of the Prime Minister's policy on agriculture and industry, the industrial plan, strive to promote domestic goods to resist foreign goods, implement the policy of enriching the country and enriching the people by promoting domestic goods, implement the industrial science, improve domestic goods, improve the lives of workers to improve the rate of production, overthrow the economic aggression of imperialism, overthrow the traitors who sell foreign goods, overthrow the foreign slaves who buy foreign goods, and overthrow the treacherous merchants who destroy the workers for no reason. Long live the Chinese Kuomintang! Shanghai Special Municipal Cotton Textile Workers' Union, Zhabei District Trade Union, Pudong District Trade Union, Qiming Factory Trade Union, Hongyu Factory Trade Union.

Dispute over Short Weight in Rice Shops 122

The Social Bureau Sent Personnel to Investigate

Xin Wenyao, manager of the Chunyuan Pig Shop in Nanshi, submitted a report to the Social Bureau, saying, "Report for the purpose of rice shops deducting weight and illegally profiting, requesting review and legal action. My shop's rice has always been connected with Yang Shilin, a runner of the Tongdexiang Rice Shop outside Dananmen Street. Because my shop provides meals for the customers of the investment firm, it needs about 15 dan of rice per month. Since the transaction in February of this year, it has been four or five months. Only the first time the rice came, the chef found no shortage after reporting. Afterwards, relying on the initial credibility, the rice that came had not been reported again. Yesterday, it happened that the shop sent four dan of No. 2 rice (each dan is 20 foreign dollars) to the shop. Xin Wenyao, the manager of my shop, ordered the director to report together. Unexpectedly, the weight was greatly lacking, and it was estimated that each bag was short of more than ten jin, with a total shortage of more than eighty jin, worth about more than ten yuan. Based on this calculation, the monthly loss is 37 yuan, and the half-year loss is 450 yuan. Based on the fact that the transaction has been four full months, the loss is 150 yuan in silver. I will not trace the past transactions. I immediately telegraphed Yang Shilin, the runner of the shop, to check at the shop. Knowing that he could not hide it, he begged to return the funds. My shop believes that this kind of fraudulent situation greatly violates the principle of business, which is based on credibility, and its practices are extremely harmful to the society and the common people. At the time when rice is expensive and rice is eaten, this kind of rice shop that exploits the common people should be severely punished. I sincerely hope that the punishment will be fully appropriated to the public and the losses of the common people will be compensated. In the future, if any similar situation is found in rice shops throughout the city, it can be handled in the same way to fill the market and benefit the common people. It is a very good law. I hereby report the situation of the shop deducting the weight of rice and illegally profiting. I sincerely request your Majesty to review the matter and quickly send personnel to investigate and deal with it in accordance with the law. It is for the public good. Sincerely presented to the Director of the Social Bureau, Pan." The Social Bureau then issued Instruction No. 2436 to the Jia Guxia Rice Industry Association, saying that it was ordered to comply with the matter. Chunyuan Pig Shop Manager Xin Wenyao reported that the Tongdexiang Rice Shop outside Dananmen was deducting weight and illegally profiting, and requested that personnel be sent to investigate and deal with it in accordance with the law. Based on this, Wei Zhiping and Rong Huiren were sent to investigate. The association immediately sent personnel to investigate and report together for verification. This is the order.

Issuing Certificates for Cota Western Medicine 123

The Shanghai New Medicine Industry Association sent a letter to the Business Reorganization Association requesting proof that the Cota Western Medicine Factory is a domestic business. Yesterday, the certificate issued by the Business Reorganization Association was received as follows: For the sake of proof, it was found that Cota Western Medicine Factory, a member of the Shanghai New Medicine Industry Association, specializes in manufacturing malt extract, cod liver oil, and various medicines. In October of the 16th year, it registered with the former Agricultural and Commercial Bureau of this city in accordance with the Commercial Registration Regulations and obtained a license. In April of the 19th year, the Trademark Bureau was approved to register the trademark and issue a certificate, which has been published in the Trademark Gazette No. 33. The above two items are sufficient to prove that the pharmacy was established by a Chinese merchant and that the various goods it produces are indeed domestic goods. According to the above two points, the association requested to be given a certificate for compliance. The association believes that the nature of the pharmacy is sufficient to prove that the pharmacy has a commercial registration license and a trademark registration certificate from the former Agricultural and Commercial Bureau and the Trademark Bureau. Page 15

Local news two

Accusation of Extortion Against Detectives 126

Wu Changji has accused Hongkou Police Station detectives Cao Jie, Xu Wenzhong, Chen Bingsheng, and Chen Zhitong from Jiangbei of extortion. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Ge Zhiqin of the Special District Court opened a hearing to investigate. According to Wu Changji's testimony, Tang Fujiji and Yuan Linji, both from Jiangbei, had a dispute over money on the 3rd of this month at the Changle Teahouse on Fuzhou Road. Wu Changji mediated the dispute at the scene. Around 4 PM, detectives Cao, Xu, and Chen Bingsheng suddenly arrived and took him to the Hongkou Police Station, accusing him of attempting to pickpocket someone. Later, his friend Chen Zhitong came to visit, and after a long negotiation with the three detectives, Wu Changji was released. The detectives allegedly told Chen Zhitong that they needed 250 yuan for entertainment expenses. Chen Zhitong informed Wu Changji, who agreed and paid the money to Chen Zhitong on the 5th. Wu Changji stated that he did not know what happened after that. Chen Zhitong then testified that Wu Changji was his foster son. After Wu Changji was detained, he visited him and negotiated with Detective Cao to pay 250 yuan for his release. However, when it came to paying the money, the detectives refused to accept it because of concerns about rumors. Xu Wenzhong testified that on the 3rd of this month, he and detectives Cao and Chen saw Wu Changji acting suspiciously at the Changle Teahouse, so they took him back to the Hongkou Police Station and reported it to Western Detective Captain Clatten, asking if Wu Changji had any witnesses to prove his good behavior. Wu Changji then mentioned Chen Zhitong, so they summoned Chen Zhitong. Xu Wenzhong also went to Wu Changji's residence at the Shanban Factory New Bridge to investigate and found no evidence of bad conduct. Captain Clatten then ordered Wu Changji's release. On the 6th, Detective Cao invited Xu Wenzhong to a banquet, and on the way, they met Chen Zhitong, who offered him 250 yuan, which Xu Wenzhong refused to accept. Xu Wenzhong stated that he had not solicited a bribe beforehand. The testimonies of detectives Cao and Chen were largely similar to Xu's. Captain Clatten reported that the three detectives had taken Wu Changji to the police station, initially suspecting him of being a pickpocket. He had intended to accompany the detectives to Wu Changji's home to investigate, but a fire broke out at 147 Wusong Road, and he had to go to the fire scene. Upon returning to the police station, he found Xu Wenzhong in the office, who reported that Chen Zhitong could vouch for Wu Changji's character. After questioning Chen Zhitong, Wu Changji was released due to lack of evidence of a crime. Other witnesses also testified, and lawyers from the police station and defense lawyers Jiang Yiping and Fan Gang debated the matter. Judge Ge adjourned the hearing and announced that the verdict would be delivered on the afternoon of the 29th of this month.

Accusation of Bribery Against Police Officers 127

Possession of Concealed Firearm Leads to Five-Year Sentence

Bribery Allegations to Be Further Investigated

At 10 PM last night, Chinese police officers Li Zhaobang (No. 2084) and another officer (No. 1356) from the Xinzha Police Station arrested Yong Ren Wang Yinhu and confiscated a handgun with seven live rounds. They reported to the police chief that they had seen Wang acting suspiciously at the intersection of Datong Road and Xinzha Road, heading west. They attempted to search him, but he fled. They chased him into the Xin Kang Lane, where Wang allegedly drew the gun and attempted to resist arrest. Li fired two shots, and the other officer fired one shot, after which Wang surrendered. No one was injured by the shots. The police chief questioned Wang Yinhu, who claimed that Little Mapi ordered him to take the handgun to the small vegetable market. He was arrested while passing Suzhou Road. Officer Li demanded 300 yuan as a bribe for his release, and Wang agreed, but since he had no money, Officer Li fired three shots and then took him to the police station. Wang claimed that the officers' report did not match the facts. The police chief ordered Chinese detective Tao Rubi and Western detective Mai Fali to investigate. The detectives found three shell casings near Datong Road and Suzhou Road, which were identified as bullets issued to the two officers. However, the location of the casings was about 150 yards away from the location reported by the officers. Since both officers had already left work, the detectives went to their homes, brought them back to the police station, and interrogated them severely. Officer No. 1356 eventually admitted that they had apprehended Wang near Suzhou Road and fired shots. The police chief, believing that the officers had made a dishonest report, confiscated their weapons. Yesterday morning, Wang Yinhu and the two officers were sent to the Special District Court, where Judge Wu held a hearing. After the Chinese and Western detectives reported the investigation, the two officers denied the bribery allegations. Wang maintained that he was carrying the gun to the vegetable market for Little Mapi and was arrested on the way. The police officer demanded 300 yuan for his release, but he was taken to the police station because he had no money. After the hearing, Judge Wu immediately sentenced Wang Yinhu to five years in prison for possessing military firearms for criminal purposes, and the handgun and ammunition were confiscated. The bribery allegations against Li Zhaobang will be investigated separately.

Child Kidnapping Foiled by Father 129

Xu Baohong's Scheme Exposed

Zhang Kangming, a rickshaw puller from Yancheng residing at 352 Manzhou Road in Zhabei, is 47 years old and has only one son, Xiao Liuwen, who is only six years old. The boy has delicate features and is well-loved. Zhang and his wife cherish him dearly. At around 6 PM the day before yesterday, Xiao Liuwen was playing in front of their house when he was approached by a kidnapper from Funing, Xu Baohong, who used candy as bait. Xiao Liuwen, being young and naive, took the candy. Xu then lied, saying, "I'll take you to eat sweets." Xiao Liuwen believed him and was carried by Xu towards the New Update Stage. Coincidentally, Zhang Kangming, the boy's father, was returning home from the concession when he saw a stranger carrying his beloved son. He questioned Xu, who tried to flee, abandoning the child. Zhang grabbed him and handed him over to officer Shi Qingxiang at the No. 1 precinct of the Fourth District. Zhang's wife had also reported the missing child to the police station. After questioning by Chief Yao, Xu Baohong claimed that he was not trying to kidnap the child but had noticed the gold lock and necklace around the child's neck and intended to take him to a secluded place to steal them. Chief Yao, finding Xu's statement to be an attempt to downplay the crime of child abduction, submitted a report to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Lawyer Xi's Lawsuit

Settlement of Ma's Breach of Contract Case 131

Compensation of 150 Yuan

Apology to Xi

The Jinlingchun Restaurant on Zhengjia Bridge, a vegetable restaurant, is owned by the Ma family of Nanjing. The owner has five brothers, with the eldest, Ma Houji, managing the family affairs. His widowed sister-in-law, Ms. Ma, previously engaged lawyer Xi Yaofu to negotiate with Ma Houji because he did not distribute the property according to the late Mr. Ma's will. Initially, she lacked funds for legal fees and entered into a contract with lawyer Xi, stating that she would pay 30% of the recovered property as compensation. The amount in dispute was nearly ten thousand. Later, lawyer Xi was unable to reach a peaceful resolution and filed a lawsuit on her behalf. However, Ms. Ma settled with Ma Houji independently and denied that she had authorized Xi to file the lawsuit. Xi believed that Ms. Ma had broken her word and profited at his expense and was unjustly slandering him, which was intolerable. Therefore, he engaged two lawyers, Zhao Chuanding and others, to sue Ms. Ma and the guarantors of the contract, demanding the fulfillment of the contract. Yesterday morning, the Special District Court held a hearing. The plaintiff's lawyer stated that lawyer Xi had put in a lot of effort to handle the case for the defendant and only received 50 yuan for office expenses. The defendant had reconciled without informing Xi and then claimed that she had not entrusted Xi to file the lawsuit, which was unacceptable. Xi did not care about the compensation but felt that she was too untrustworthy and should apologize. The defendant, Ms. Ma, hired lawyer Shan Yuhua to defend her and expressed her willingness to settle with the plaintiff. Judge Yang Yi also advised both parties to settle. As a result, the defendant agreed to compensate the plaintiff 150 yuan for public expenses within seven days and to issue a statement to lawyer Xi expressing her misunderstanding and regret.

Worker Crushed to Death by Cotton Bales 132

Shen Sannian, a worker from Jiangbei who worked for the Huafu Company on Huaji Road in Hongkou, was nearing thirty years of age. On the day before yesterday (the 11th), he was dispatched by the company to the Osaka Wharf to load a large batch of cotton bales. The goods had already been loaded when Shen, while arranging things on the truck, was crushed by a heavy cotton bale that rolled down, breaking his left arm and rendering him unconscious. He was sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment, but his injuries were too severe, and he died in the hospital at around 2 PM yesterday.

Robbery Case on Zilai Street, Thieves Tried and Sentenced 133

Six robbers broke into Zheng Qianqing's Zheng Qiaji store at 12 Shenxing Lane, Zilai Street, in the French Concession, on the evening of the 21st of last month and stole over 1,300 silver dollars. The details were reported previously. Detectives Lu Jinchen, Lu Jinbao, and Bao Tan Jiang Changwen, Gu Zhou Zhixiang and others from the French Concession police station, discovered where the robbers were hiding and immediately arrested them. The robbers were Yang Asan, Zhang Songlin, Chen Ruifu, Shen Hongchu, Shen Jinfu, and the female thief Chen Wubao. They confiscated three handguns and 300 yuan of the stolen money. They were brought to the police station and handed over to the French Court for prosecution. The plaintiff, Zheng Qianqing, stated that the defendants came to rob his store three times. The first time, they were discovered by merchants who rang the alarm bell, causing the robbers to flee in fear. The second time, a student blew a whistle, causing them to flee. This was their third attempt, and they were caught off guard, leading to the robbery. He requested that they be severely punished. Yang Asan, Zhang Songlin, Chen Ruifu, and Shen Hongchu confessed that Zhang Asi, who is still at large, instigated them to commit the robbery. Shen Jinfu confessed that he went to attempt the robbery the first time but was not present during the second and third robberies, and he asked for leniency. Chen Wubao confessed that she was in a relationship with Chen Ruifu and was unaware of the robbery. The other defendants gave evasive answers. The Western detective chief reported that the third defendant, Chen Ruifu, had previously been sentenced to five years in prison for robbery and then sent to the mainland court for trial, but he did not know how he was released. He has now committed another crime and has been arrested. He requested that he be severely punished. Judge Zhu, with the approval of the French Consul, sentenced Yang Asan, Zhang Songlin, Chen Ruifu, and Shen Hongchu to five years each in the Western Prison, followed by deportation to the mainland authorities for trial. Chen Wubao was deported. The handguns were confiscated, and the stolen money was returned to the plaintiff.

After the election of the second committee of the Shanghai Special Municipality Chinese Medicine Association, the first joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees was held the other day. Xie Liheng chaired the meeting, and Yu Qinzhai recorded the minutes. Cai Jiping and Jiang Wenfang proposed: (A) To maintain the business of the members and develop the efficacy of medicines, the following six sub-items were proposed: 1. The association should establish an academic lecture hall and hold regular lectures several times a month to enhance the intelligence of the members. 2. The association should establish several consultation clinics where members can request consultations for major diseases to ensure thoroughness. 3. Organize and rectify the Discipline Committee of the industry to maintain the ethics of the industry. It was decided to hand it over to the organization section for planning and implementation. 4. When requesting the court to hear cases of unauthorized accusations against members, pay attention to Articles 180, 330, and 370 of the Criminal Law to deter fraud and false accusations and protect business credit. 5. Send a letter to newspapers requesting that they do not rush to publish cases of unauthorized accusations against doctors before the verdict is announced, let alone use headlines such as "Incompetent Doctors Killing People" to respect human rights. 6. Issue a declaration explaining that unauthorized accusations against doctors should not only be subject to criminal penalties but also make doctors unwilling to treat serious illnesses, which is detrimental to the general public. It was decided to hand it over to the secretariat for handling. (B) To expand the organization of the association, the following three sub-items were proposed: 1. Hand over to the executive committee to determine the location and appoint soliciting members to organize a soliciting team. 2. Those who join the association within two months from the start of the solicitation members will be exempted from the membership fee. 3. Add preparatory members. Those in the same industry who do not meet the qualifications in Article 6, Item A of the association's charter may pre-join the association and enjoy membership rights once their qualifications are complete. It was decided to hand it over to the organization section for handling. (C) Send a letter to medical academic groups requesting financial assistance for the association. It was decided that the standing committee would contact them first before sending a letter. (D) Xu Shoupeng proposed the establishment of consultation and inquiry departments. It was decided to incorporate it into case A for handling. (E) Xi Xiaowu proposed the construction of the association building. It was decided to hand it over to the finance section for planning. (F) Guo Boliang proposed that the association print and issue trust letters to patients to provide security. It was decided to approve it in principle, and the secretariat was invited to negotiate the method with the original proposer. (G) Ding Zhongying moved that should preparatory members be reported for registration on their behalf? Gong Hanwen added that those who directly register and receive licenses without being reviewed by the trial committee should be investigated. It was decided that the reporting of registration on their behalf was approved, and Gong's supplementary case was handed over to the standing committee for handling. (H) Jiang Wenfang moved to form an economic committee, a construction committee, and a social committee, and to invite medical experts to serve as members to expand the association's affairs. It was decided to hand it over to the standing committee to draw up a list and submit it to the executive committee for approval and implementation.

Free Talk

A Word or Two 144

A woman is a spiritual magnet for a man, so a man will often stand still when he sees a woman.

A teacher can teach you to read, but not everyone can see the depths of the subject. Love has no instructor, yet everyone knows how to ask for directions.

The more shy a woman is, the more men admire her, because a woman's shyness truly has a mysterious beauty. A woman looking at a man with a hint of intention can drive him wild. A man looking at a woman like a hawk or a hungry tiger can terrify her.

Cohabitation is the end of love and the beginning of troubles. If you can often think about what is in your own heart, you will naturally offend fewer people.

If everyone wants to achieve their ideal of a beautiful wife, concubine, Western-style house, and car by pursuing advanced knowledge, then national universities can be closed down, and government-funded students can be discontinued.

If you invent a science, you might as well announce it to the public so that they can admire you. If you find a new lover, it is best to keep it a secret for now.

The handwriting and wording of a love letter must be ten times more genuine than a letter to your parents if you want to have any hope of receiving a reply.

When writing a letter, it is better to be quick, but when sealing a letter, it is better to be slow, lest you accidentally seal a letter intended for Miss B in the letter to Miss A, causing a major scandal.

"Mourning Snow" by Canglang Jushi on Wu 145

"Mourning Snow" is an elegy by Wu people for the late Jiangsu Governor Cheng Xuelou. Xuelou's name was Dequan, also known as Suyuan Jushi. In his early years, he served as an official in Heilongjiang, where he was known at home and abroad for his loyalty, courage, and love for the people. Later, he was promoted to Governor of Jiangsu, where his diligence and pragmatism were evident. During the 1911 Revolution, Xuelou resolutely responded and eventually succeeded. The people of Wu praised him in the streets and alleys, saying, "Suzhou's restoration, we will never forget Governor Cheng." In the second year of the Republic of China, after retiring from official life, he went to Tianning Temple in Changzhou to be ordained, taking the Dharma name Xianhui. Later, he became the abbot of Fayun Temple in Mudu, immersing himself in Buddhist studies. In April of this year, he went to Shanghai for medical treatment and passed away on the 29th. In his will, he ordered that no obituary be issued, no funeral be held, and that he be buried as soon as possible. Before his death, Master Xue saw the decline of Hanshan Temple and the dilapidated walls and made great efforts to repair it. He also built a tomb near the temple at Banmu Bridge. Now, his coffin is scheduled to be transported to Suzhou on the 16th. The people of Wu, not forgetting his political virtues, have specially held a memorial service to express their condolences. The memorial service was held at Baoji Temple in the city on the 10th. More than 100 members of the association came, half of them from Ning, Hu, Zhen, and Xi, and those who had a connection with Cheng were all dressed in plain carriages and white horses, which was a grand occasion. Zhuang Yunkuan, Chen Taoyi, Chen Qicai, Luo Liangjian, Huang Yanpei, Shen Sifu, Zhang Yilin, Fei Shuwei, and others all wrote elegiac couplets to come for this grand affair.

Shen Si wrote: "Gengzi, why did you come from the north, Xinhai, why did you come from the south? Compassion is all you had to offer. All worldly desires swept away by the tide, where now is Yongkang, where now is Nantong? After countless changes, people now know."

Shen wrote: "From ancient times the four elements have been empty, the deceased has left as if this was understood. The Buddha's teachings say there is no rebirth, of the ancients love remains and will always leave their mark. One can mourn those like Yang Gong over the fallen tears of a monument."

The Jiangsu Provincial Government also had a couplet that said: "The banner of righteousness was raised in the three Wus, relying on your shielding of the southeast. The mountains and lakes have not been subjected to the ravages of time. The wonderful sound participates in the six dharmas, proving the fruit of enlightenment. The cranes will welcome you to the Trayastrimsa Heaven."

During the ceremony, Zhang Yilin presided over the sacrifice, with solemn rituals and mournful music. Zhang also stated the major events in Cheng Gong's life and his sincere love for the people and the country, with his voice choked with tears. Yuan Xiluo, the magistrate of Taicang County, also gave a speech, detailing how Cheng's merits in building the country were sufficient to be a model for us. His words were particularly tragic. After the ceremony, a photograph was taken, and commemorative round badges were distributed, with Cheng's portrait printed in the middle and the words "Xianhui" inscribed on it.

Common Sense Scraps from Wu Shan 146

When we eat too quickly, hiccups often occur. Ordinary people only know to drink good tea to relieve them, but they don't know that if you mix sugar with vinegar and eat it, the hiccups can be immediately relieved, because vinegar's property of regulating qi is better than any other item.

During hot weather, foul odors most easily occur in ditches, and small insects breed, which is a great hindrance to hygiene. But if we can sprinkle a few gallons of kerosene into it, this trouble can be avoided, because kerosene is rich in insecticidal power and deodorizing effect, so sprinkling it is most beneficial.

When it's hot, candles melt easily, which is quite uneconomical. But if you can sprinkle a little salt on them when burning, not only can you avoid the trouble of melting, but the light of the candle will also be doubled as a result.

The remains of the old monk Cheng Gong Xuelou" After the adjournment, it was heard that there were still offerings from abbots of various temples and elders of various mountains, which was also a great ritual of public sacrifice outside the realm.

Rambling Talk on Water Chestnuts by Zheng Yimei 147

Water chestnuts are between fruits and vegetables. Eating them tastes clear and elegant, like reading the poetry of Wei Suzhou. People in Shanghai call them "ground chestnuts," and people in Guangdong call them "horse hooves." In ancient times, they also had the aliases "Wu Yu" and "Fu Ci." Fu Ci is found in the Erya, so their origin is very ancient. However, ancient people rarely sang about them, so they are not listed in encyclopedias, probably because there are no historical facts about them.

Water chestnuts are produced in paddy fields. In early spring, seeds are kept, waiting for sprouts to grow, and then they are buried in mud jars. After two or three months, they are transplanted back into paddy fields. The stems are about three feet high, hollow like tubes, tender and green, and very lovely. The flower spikes gather at the ends of the stems. The so-called water chestnuts are the tubers under the ground.

In Wansu Village outside the Feng Gate of my Suzhou, the water chestnuts produced are black. In Hualin, the water chestnuts produced are red. They are all sweet and tender in taste and are famous products.

In Nanchang, Jiangxi, even more water chestnuts are produced, with a lot of sweet juice. It is said that they cannot be dropped on the ground, as they will immediately become crushed and irreparable. Their tenderness is evident.

If you have ringworm on your face, you can scrape a water chestnut and rub it on it several times, and it will heal. Also, if you accidentally swallow an old-style coin, eating water chestnuts can help the coin pass, as they have a bowel-lubricating effect.

In summer, there is a cold snack called "water chestnut jelly," but in fact, there is no water chestnut in the jelly. The juice is actually a type of jelly.

When eating water chestnuts, there is the trouble of peeling them. Therefore, street vendors shave them and string them together for sale, called "polished water chestnuts." They are white and tender like lard and incomparably refreshing. However, vendors often soak them in cold water, which is not hygienic.

Water chestnuts do not rot easily and can be hung in baskets under the eaves to wait for them to dry. After drying, the skin wrinkles and is easy to peel, and the taste is even sweeter. Some people also boil them and eat them, which is also quite delicious.

The color of water chestnuts is red and translucent. Lacquered wooden objects with a red and translucent color are therefore called "water chestnut lacquer."

In the custom of Wu, one water chestnut must be placed in the rice grains when eating New Year's Eve dinner, called "digging for hidden wealth," which is truly laughable.

There is a sugar shop in Wu called "Wild Water Chestnut," which is quite famous. According to legend, when building the house, a particularly large and unusual wild water chestnut was dug up underground. Therefore, the shop name was immediately named "Wild Water Chestnut." The wild water chestnut that was dug up was offered in the cabinets, and for a time, it was widely spread, and the business flourished greatly. It is also a well-established shop in Wu.

Travel Notes from Nanyang (29) Spiritual Flowers 149

Twenty, I visited a rubber factory with hundreds of male and female workers. Female workers are paid cheaply, now only four or five corners, male workers six or seven corners. But in the past, wages were high, but now the price has been reduced because the rubber is cheap. The smell in the rubber manufacturing place is very bad and very unsuitable for hygiene. We dare not stay for a long time, but the housing of the capitalists is like heaven. The male and female workers in this factory are also human beings. They work hard day and night in the midst of bad air, and the few corners they earn, that is, when the price of rubber was expensive in the past, the capitalists had already made a fortune. Now that the price of rubber is low, the workers alone suffer the losses. It is not a fair matter.

Twenty-one, I visited a friend and talked about the economic situation. According to the exchange house, Singapore has about 400,000 Chinese. In the past, the amount of money remitted to China every day could be 800,000, but recently, due to the decline in commerce, it is only 400,000 to 500,000 per day. That is, on average, each person remits one yuan to China every day, which is also 400,000 per day. From this calculation, it can be estimated that this one port alone remits more than ten million yuan back to China every month, and still one or two hundred million yuan per year. Therefore, the contribution of overseas Chinese to the national economy is not small.

Twenty-two, I discussed the issue of Nanyang clothing. The clothing of the natives of Nanyang is extremely simple, and even the Chinese here mostly wear white cloth clothes and rarely wear silk. The same is true for women, which is not the slightest bit a leak in the sales of foreign goods. I think that Chinese silk clothing should be promoted to suit the summer. This is also an important matter. I hope that the domestic silk industry will organize propaganda groups to come to Nanyang to promote it, because silk is not suitable for winter but is suitable for non-winter. The hundreds of millions of overseas Chinese in various parts of Nanyang all have the power to wear silk. Why abandon the most suitable, beautiful, and hygienic silk and listen to its decline, while contributing money to foreigners with Western cloth? Wealthy Chinese people do not wear silk but wear foreign yarn. This is abandoning their noble status and demeaning themselves, abandoning our inherent beauty and taking ugliness, abandoning refinement and taking roughness. I very much hope that the domestic silk industry will organize a large propaganda group to save the silk industry. If they seize this large market and do not promote it overseas, and sit and let it be overwhelmed by rough foreign yarn, then the silk industry will be foolish and ignorant of business conditions, and the general traitors who demean themselves by wearing foreign cloth will do so. As for saying that they advocate democracy and therefore do not wear silk, this is a deceiving statement. If you truly advocate democracy, you should run civilian factories, education, and public welfare undertakings, and be willing to spend your surplus profits to fill public welfare, not be stingy. As for Buddhists not wearing silk to avoid killing, this is a minor matter. Can we stop the fishing industry and farmers from destroying pests because of this? This is an unchanging superstition that is not worth discussing national economy and people's livelihood with. The exhibition results are outstanding and impressive, especially the Twenty-Four Filial Piety Pictures, which belong to elementary schools, so that the fundamental family education is instilled in the brains of young students. Its intention is extremely appropriate and admirable. I also presented a small vertical scroll with the words "The essence of the country, the light of Southern Chu, only Qunyi does not yield to Yuanxiang."

Mr. Chen Menglu of Haiyan, the embroidery exhibition has six rooms, full of beautiful things, vertical scrolls, couplets, screens, square pieces, all kinds of calligraphy and painting are prepared, and supplemented with practical items, all from the embroidery work. Especially the figure embroidery and the sketch embroidery are particularly good. It is almost the so-called "the magic wants to reach the tip of the autumn hair, and the tailoring eliminates the traces of needle and thread". Therefore, I composed two short poems to leave a mark. The sentences say: "Peach and plum spring breeze flourish, the door and wall are nourished by timely rain. The five-patterned diligent woman's work, the four virtues save the world. The elegant and ingenious needle reputation, the true can be thin customs and doctors. Ascend to the hall for a browse, the colorful and happy scattered. The vitality contains the vitality, the magic reaches the tip of the hair. The golden needle to save the world, the shocking wooden bell announces. Yuan Song Gan Liao hard to carry, Li Yan Xin biography. Press the line, sigh, I am tired, the incense petals wish."

Mr. Huang Taixuan collected the true works of famous people in ancient times and contemporary masterpieces, all of which were produced in the Pingyuan method of silk embroidery. It is felt that there is still an antique charm in the dazzling light of jewelry, which is noble. It is not only the achievement of Jia Ye.

Mr. Gu Xuhou of the Commercial Press said that the art of embroidery is not what I know. Visiting the rooms, the results are uniform, elegant, neat, lively, and lovely. The materials are either historical materials, such as the Twenty-Four Filial Piety, which is helpful to popular education, or ornamental items, such as landscapes and figures, all of which are lively and interesting, or valuable items, such as pillows, bedding, and clothing, which are bright and dazzling. Flowers and birds are vividly portrayed. Adorned with the pens of talented scholars, the ingenuity of women's bodies is managed. Warmth in My Heart (222) Bao Tianxiao 150

Chapter 12 Farewell banquet, farewell, and leave a beautiful shadow. Garden grand gathering, tea competition, and appreciation of beauty.

Who knew that after passing through the gate, there was a completely different realm. This master actually had a mother, and the whole family called her the old lady. The old lady was very strict in managing the family. Even if the master made a mistake, the old lady would also reprimand him. As long as the old lady was angry, the son would have to kneel on the ground. How could many concubines not kneel down when the master knelt down? So at that time, there was a dark crowd kneeling in a room. However, although the old lady's family education was strict, she allowed her son to take concubines. She said that it was appropriate for officials and government officials to take three wives and four concubines, but after taking them, they had to live in the large mansion and were not allowed to rent small houses outside. Whenever a concubine entered the house, the first thing she did was to see the old lady and kowtow. After kowtowing, the old lady would give a speech, especially to the girls who were taken from the brothel. The old lady said, "Now you are leaving a life of prostitution and becoming a family member. Family members have the rules of family members. From now on, you must turn over a new leaf." Moreover, in our mansion, there is no need to dress up enchantingly. For example, if you have rubbed powder and applied rouge, immediately bring a basin of face water and force you to wash off the finger powder. For example, if you have kept bangs, immediately teach you to comb your bangs up. If you can't comb them up, she calls a barber to shave off your bangs. Whatever hairstyle is difficult to look at, such as the horizontal Ace head or the vertical Ace head, is not allowed in this mansion. You must comb the same ingot bun as the old lady. All fashionable clothes must be changed. That kind of small waist and big trouser legs is a vixen's dress, not right, not right. She issues a set of red cotton-padded jackets and lined cotton leggings for you to wear. Originally, this master's ancestral home was in the north. Young northern wives wear red and green. Do you think those Shanghai girls who like to show off would be willing to wear that kind of clothes? Even the southern girls in the northern alleys have never worn that set of clothes. If you say you don't want to, now that we have spent a lot of money to buy you here, you are a member of our mansion, and everything must follow the rules of our mansion and cannot be self-assertive. If you cry and don't want to, put you in an empty room and lock you up for a year or two. By then, you will naturally be submissive and dare not have any more wild ambitions. I heard that there were many who committed suicide because of this, but people who were bought with money are not worth anything when they die. The death of one person is only the death of a dog. The master has many concubines and does not care about one or two. However, the people of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces who talk about humanitarianism treat their concubines much more favorably. However, people who come from brothels are inevitably fickle and drift with the wind, but they cannot but be guarded against.

The Reason for the Tightening and Loosening of the Money Supply 155

According to a recent conversation with people in the financial world, the previous tightening of the money supply was purely due to people's panic. In fact, there is no possibility of money tightening when silver is cheap. When the previous gold price surge was very strong, there were many people in the general financial world who speculated in gold and foreign exchange and suffered losses. Therefore, the outside world spread rumors of mutual infighting, so the money supply was tightened. This gold price surge will come to an end, and the market will gradually stabilize, and the money supply will loosen accordingly.

Therefore, it is difficult for new factories to transfer the price via telegram. Chinese silk merchants have higher silk costs and excessive losses, making it difficult to sell. The market has become a rejected situation. Old silk is not moving through England and France, and US sales are also stagnant, tending to be depressed. The future of the foreign firm silk market is becoming increasingly dangerous.

North-South Goods Longkou Vermicelli Inventory Shortage, Rising Half a Liang 168

Longkou thin vermicelli previously fell to 18 taels due to a lack of sales, but recently the price has risen by 3 qian due to inventory shortages and increased sales. According to a letter from the area, the price has also risen. Due to the high cost, the market price has risen from 18 taels 3 qian to 18 taels and a half. Those with relatively thin inventories are waiting and watching, and do not intend to sell. The trend may become tense again.
